pipeline migration:  parse binlog error when JSON column in increment task 
### Which version of ShardingSphere did you use?

5.5.3-SNAPSHOT

### Which project did you use? ShardingSphere-JDBC or ShardingSphere-Proxy?

 ShardingSphere-Proxy

### Expected behavior

Binlog parser should correctly handle JSON columns containing the literal value 'null'

### Actual behavior

**Binlog parser throws UnsupportedSQLOperationException when encountering a MySQL JSON column containing the literal string value 'null'**

Error occurs with this sequence:


CREATE TABLE  reproduce_json_parse_error (
   id bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  settlement_assets json NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (id)
);

INSERT INTO reproduce_json_parse_error(settlement_assets) VALUES('null');

**Error message:**
org.apache.shardingsphere.infra.exception.generic.UnsupportedSQLOperationException: Unsupported SQL operation: 4

### More 

- When the parsing error occurs, the binlog client becomes corrupted

- Current implementation attempts to skip the error event but fails to properly skip unresolved bytes

- This causes incorrect parsing of subsequent events

    18	package org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.value.string;
    19	
    20	import io.netty.buffer.ByteBuf;
    21	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.MySQLBinlogColumnDef;
    22	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.value.MySQLBinlogProtocolValue;
    23	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.payload.MySQLPacketPayload;
    24	import org.apache.shardingsphere.infra.exception.generic.UnsupportedSQLOperationException;
    25	
    26	import java.io.Serializable;
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * JSON type value of MySQL binlog protocol.
    30	 *
    31	 * <p>
    32	 *     There are no detail document about JSON type in MySQL replication.
    33	 *     Also no detail document in MariaDB.
    34	 *     Decoding implementation is referred to MySQL source code.
    35	 * </p>
    36	 *
    37	 * @see <a href="https://github.com/mysql/mysql-server/blob/5.7/sql/json_binary.h">json_binary</a>
    38	 */
    39	public final class MySQLJsonBinlogProtocolValue implements MySQLBinlogProtocolValue {
    40	    
    41	    @Override
    42	    public Serializable read(final MySQLBinlogColumnDef columnDef, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    43	        ByteBuf newlyByteBuf = payload.getByteBuf().readBytes(readLengthFromMeta(columnDef.getColumnMeta(), payload));
    44	        try {
    45	            return MySQLJsonValueDecoder.decode(newlyByteBuf);
    46	        } finally {
    47	            newlyByteBuf.release();
    48	        }
    49	    }
    50	    
    51	    private int readLengthFromMeta(final int columnMeta, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    52	        switch (columnMeta) {
    53	            case 1:
    54	                return payload.getByteBuf().readUnsignedByte();
    55	            case 2:
    56	                return payload.getByteBuf().readUnsignedShortLE();
    57	            case 3:
    58	                return payload.getByteBuf().readUnsignedMediumLE();
    59	            case 4:
    60	                return payload.readInt4();
    61	            default:
    62	                throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.format("MySQL JSON type meta in binlog should be range 1 to 4, but actual value is: %s", columnMeta));
    63	        }
    64	    }
    65	}

    18	package org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.value.string;
    19	
    20	import io.netty.buffer.ByteBuf;
    21	import lombok.AccessLevel;
    22	import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
    23	import org.apache.shardingsphere.infra.exception.generic.UnsupportedSQLOperationException;
    24	
    25	import java.io.Serializable;
    26	import java.math.BigInteger;
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * JSON type value decoder for MySQL.
    30	 *
    31	 * @see <a href="https://github.com/mysql/mysql-server/blob/5.7/sql/json_binary.h">json_binary</a>
    32	 */
    33	@NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PRIVATE)
    34	public final class MySQLJsonValueDecoder {
    35	    
    36	    private static final BigInteger MAX_BIG_INTEGER_VALUE = new BigInteger("18446744073709551615");
    37	    
    38	    /**
    39	     * Decode mysql json binary data to json string.
    40	     *
    41	     * @param byteBuf json binary value payload
    42	     * @return json string
    43	     */
    44	    public static Serializable decode(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
    45	        int valueType = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte() & 0xff;
    46	        StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
    47	        decodeValue(valueType, 1, byteBuf, result);
    48	        return result.toString();
    49	    }
    50	    
    51	    private static void decodeValue(final int type, final int offset, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
    52	        int oldOffset = byteBuf.readerIndex();
    53	        byteBuf.readerIndex(offset);
    54	        try {
    55	            switch (type) {
    56	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT:
    57	                    decodeJsonObject(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    58	                    break;
    59	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT:
    60	                    decodeJsonObject(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    61	                    break;
    62	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:
    63	                    decodeJsonArray(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    64	                    break;
    65	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:
    66	                    decodeJsonArray(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    67	                    break;
    68	                case JsonValueTypes.INT16:
    69	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readShortLE());
    70	                    break;
    71	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT16:
    72	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE());
    73	                    break;
    74	                case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
    75	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readIntLE());
    76	                    break;
    77	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
    78	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE());
    79	                    break;
    80	                case JsonValueTypes.INT64:
    81	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readLongLE());
    82	                    break;
    83	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:
    84	                    stringBuilder.append(readUnsignedLongLE(byteBuf));
    85	                    break;
    86	                case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:
    87	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readDoubleLE());
    88	                    break;
    89	                case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
    90	                    outputString(decodeString(byteBuf.slice()), stringBuilder);
    91	                    break;
    92	                default:
    93	                    throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));
    94	            }
    95	        } finally {
    96	            byteBuf.readerIndex(oldOffset);
    97	        }
    98	    }
    99	    
   100	    private static BigInteger readUnsignedLongLE(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   101	        long value = byteBuf.readLongLE();
   102	        return 0L <= value ? BigInteger.valueOf(value) : MAX_BIG_INTEGER_VALUE.add(BigInteger.valueOf(1L + value));
   103	    }
   104	    
   105	    private static void decodeJsonObject(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
   106	        stringBuilder.append('{');
   107	        int count = getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   108	        getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   109	        String[] keys = new String[count];
   110	        for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   111	            keys[i] = decodeKeyEntry(isSmall, byteBuf);
   112	        }
   113	        for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   114	            if (0 < i) {
   115	                stringBuilder.append(',');
   116	            }
   117	            stringBuilder.append('"').append(keys[i]).append("\":");
   118	            decodeValueEntry(isSmall, byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   119	        }
   120	        stringBuilder.append('}');
   121	    }
   122	    
   123	    private static void decodeJsonArray(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
   124	        stringBuilder.append('[');
   125	        int count = getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   126	        getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   127	        for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   128	            if (0 < i) {
   129	                stringBuilder.append(',');
   130	            }
   131	            decodeValueEntry(isSmall, byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   132	        }
   133	        stringBuilder.append(']');
   134	    }
   135	    
   136	    private static String decodeKeyEntry(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   137	        int offset = getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   138	        int length = byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE();
   139	        byte[] data = new byte[length];
   140	        byteBuf.getBytes(offset, data, 0, length);
   141	        return new String(data);
   142	    }
   143	    
   144	    private static void decodeValueEntry(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
   145	        int type = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte() & 0xff;
   146	        switch (type) {
   147	            case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT:
   148	            case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT:
   149	            case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:
   150	            case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:
   151	            case JsonValueTypes.INT64:
   152	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:
   153	            case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:
   154	            case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
   155	                decodeValue(type, getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   156	                break;
   157	            case JsonValueTypes.INT16:
   158	                stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readShortLE());
   159	                if (!isSmall) {
   160	                    byteBuf.skipBytes(2);
   161	                }
   162	                break;
   163	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT16:
   164	                stringBuilder.append(getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall));
   165	                break;
   166	            case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
   167	                if (isSmall) {
   168	                    decodeValue(type, byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE(), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   169	                } else {
   170	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readIntLE());
   171	                }
   172	                break;
   173	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
   174	                if (isSmall) {
   175	                    decodeValue(type, byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE(), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   176	                } else {
   177	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE());
   178	                }
   179	                break;
   180	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
   181	                outputLiteral(getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall), stringBuilder);
   182	                break;
   183	            default:
   184	                throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));
   185	        }
   186	    }
   187	    
   188	    private static int getIntBasedObjectSize(final ByteBuf byteBuf, final boolean isSmall) {
   189	        return isSmall ? byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE() : (int) byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE();
   190	    }
   191	    
   192	    private static void outputLiteral(final int inlineValue, final StringBuilder out) {
   193	        switch (inlineValue) {
   194	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_NULL:
   195	                out.append("null");
   196	                break;
   197	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_TRUE:
   198	                out.append("true");
   199	                break;
   200	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_FALSE:
   201	                out.append("false");
   202	                break;
   203	            default:
   204	                throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(inlineValue));
   205	        }
   206	    }
   207	    
   208	    private static String decodeString(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   209	        int length = decodeDataLength(byteBuf);
   210	        byte[] buffer = new byte[length];
   211	        byteBuf.readBytes(buffer, 0, length);
   212	        return new String(buffer);
   213	    }
   214	    
   215	    private static int decodeDataLength(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   216	        int result = 0;
   217	        int i = 0;
   218	        while (true) {
   219	            int data = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte();
   220	            result |= (data & 0x7f) << (7 * i);
   221	            if (0 == (data & 0x80)) {
   222	                break;
   223	            }
   224	            i++;
   225	        }
   226	        return result;
   227	    }
   228	    
   229	    private static void outputString(final String str, final StringBuilder out) {
   230	        out.append('"');
   231	        for (int i = 0; i < str.length(); ++i) {
   232	            char c = str.charAt(i);
   233	            if (c == '"' || c == '\\') {
   234	                out.append('\\');
   235	            }
   236	            out.append(c);
   237	        }
   238	        out.append('"');
   239	    }
   240	    
   241	    /**
   242	     * Json value types.
   243	     */
   244	    @NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PRIVATE)
   245	    public static final class JsonValueTypes {
   246	        
   247	        public static final byte SMALL_JSON_OBJECT = 0x00;
   248	        
   249	        public static final byte LARGE_JSON_OBJECT = 0x01;
   250	        
   251	        public static final byte SMALL_JSON_ARRAY = 0x02;
   252	        
   253	        public static final byte LARGE_JSON_ARRAY = 0x03;
   254	        
   255	        /**
   256	         * Literal(true/false/null).
   257	         */
   258	        public static final byte LITERAL = 0x04;
   259	        
   260	        public static final byte LITERAL_NULL = 0x00;
   261	        
   262	        public static final byte LITERAL_TRUE = 0x01;
   263	        
   264	        public static final byte LITERAL_FALSE = 0x02;
   265	        
   266	        public static final byte INT16 = 0x05;
   267	        
   268	        public static final byte UINT16 = 0x06;
   269	        
   270	        public static final byte INT32 = 0x07;
   271	        
   272	        public static final byte UINT32 = 0x08;
   273	        
   274	        public static final byte INT64 = 0x09;
   275	        
   276	        public static final byte UINT64 = 0x0a;
   277	        
   278	        public static final byte DOUBLE = 0x0b;
   279	        
   280	        /**
   281	         * Utf8mb4 string.
   282	         */
   283	        public static final byte STRING = 0x0c;
   284	        
   285	        /**
   286	         * Custom data (any MySQL data type).
   287	         */
   288	        public static final byte CUSTOM_DATA = 0x0f;
   289	    }
   290	}

2026-05-30 04:40:05,820 - DEBUG - swea-lm-apache__shardingsphere-38622 - n_cache_control: 2
2026-05-30 04:40:21,633 - DEBUG - swea-lm-apache__shardingsphere-38622 - Response: ModelResponse(id='3f079893d2984d8fbf4b683eb49668f8', created=1780116006, model='DeepSeek-V4-Pro', object='chat.completion', system_fingerprint=None, choices=[Choices(finish_reason='tool_calls', index=0, message=Message(content='Now I understand the issue. Let me analyze:\n\n1. In `MySQLJsonValueDecoder`, the `decodeValue` method has a switch statement that handles types 0x00 through 0x0c, and the default throws `UnsupportedSQLOperationException`. \n2. Type `0x04` is `LITERAL` (null/true/false).\n3. Type `0x0f` is `CUSTOM_DATA` (any MySQL data type) - this is NOT handled.\n\nWhen a JSON column contains the literal string value \'null\' (as a string, not JSON null), MySQL stores it as a JSON string, which in the binary JSON format is type `0x0c` (STRING). Now I understand the issue. Let me analyze:

1. In `MySQLJsonValueDecoder`, the `decodeValue` method has a switch statement that handles types 0x00 through 0x0c, and the default throws `UnsupportedSQLOperationException`. 
2. Type `0x04` is `LITERAL` (null/true/false).
3. Type `0x0f` is `CUSTOM_DATA` (any MySQL data type) - this is NOT handled.

When a JSON column contains the literal string value 'null' (as a string, not JSON null), MySQL stores it as a JSON string, which in the binary JSON format is type `0x0c` (STRING). But wait, let me check: the error message says `Unsupported SQL operation: 4`. Type 4 is `LITERAL`.

Actually, looking more carefully: when you store the string 'null' in a JSON column, MySQL might store it as an opaque value (type 0x0f - CUSTOM_DATA) or as a STRING (0x0c). Let me trace through more carefully.

Wait, the error says "Unsupported SQL operation: 4". Type value 4 (0x04) is LITERAL. But that should be handled... Let me check the `decodeValueEntry` method again.

Looking at `decodeValueEntry` (line 144-186), when type is `LITERAL` (0x04), it calls `outputLiteral(getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall), stringBuilder)`. The `getIntBasedObjectSize` returns an integer that represents the literal value. The literal values are:
- 0 = null
- 1 = true
- 2 = false
- 3 = ???

But what if the value is 3 or 4? The `outputLiteral` method only handles 0, 1, 2 and throws `UnsupportedSQLOperationException` for anything else.

Now, the question is: could the literal value be 4? Let me check the MySQL source. But actually, let me re-read the PR description:

> INSERT INTO reproduce_json_parse_error(settlement_assets) VALUES('null');

So when you insert the string 'null' into a JSON column, MySQL should store it as a JSON string "null", not as a JSON null literal. But the error says "Unsupported SQL operation: 4". 

Wait, type 4 could also mean something else. Let me look at the `decodeValue` function again - the default case throws the exception with the type number. So type=4 would mean `JsonValueTypes.LITERAL` (0x04).

But `LITERAL` IS handled... unless there's a problem with how the literal value is decoded. Let me check `outputLiteral` again:

```java
case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
    outputLiteral(getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall), stringBuilder);
    break;
```

The `getIntBasedObjectSize` returns the inline value. But wait, what values can this return? According to MySQL source, for JSON literals, the inline value can be:
- 0: null
- 1: true  
- 2: false

But what about 4? Maybe there's an issue where MySQL stores the string "null" differently?

Actually, let me look at this more carefully. The issue might be about how MySQL stores JSON string "null" in binary format. In MySQL's JSON binary format, a JSON string (type 0x0c) is encoded with a variable-length length prefix followed by the string data. But if the JSON value is the literal null (not the string "null"), it's encoded as type 0x04 with inline value 0.

Wait, the error is "Unsupported SQL operation: 4". The value 4 corresponds to `JsonValueTypes.LITERAL`. But the code handles LITERAL at line 180-181. So why would it fail?

Let me look again at the `decodeValueEntry` code more carefully. At line 145:

```java
int type = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte() & 0xff;
```

And then the switch cases. What if the type is `0x04` (LITERAL)? It IS handled. But what if there's a bug in `outputLiteral`? The `getIntBasedObjectSize` returns an `int` for the literal value. If that value is something other than 0, 1, or 2, it throws the exception.

Hmm, but the error message says "Unsupported SQL operation: 4" not some other number. So the type value itself is 4.

    18	package org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.value.string;
    19	
    20	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.constant.MySQLBinaryColumnType;
    21	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.MySQLBinlogColumnDef;
    22	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.value.MySQLBinlogProtocolValue;
    23	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.payload.MySQLPacketPayload;
    24	import org.apache.shardingsphere.infra.exception.generic.UnsupportedSQLOperationException;
    25	
    26	import java.io.Serializable;
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * STRING type value of MySQL binlog protocol.
    30	 */
    31	public final class MySQLStringBinlogProtocolValue implements MySQLBinlogProtocolValue {
    32	    
    33	    @Override
    34	    public Serializable read(final MySQLBinlogColumnDef columnDef, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    35	        int type = columnDef.getColumnMeta() >> 8;
    36	        int length = columnDef.getColumnMeta() & 0xff;
    37	        // unpack type & length, see https://bugs.mysql.com/bug.php?id=37426.
    38	        if (0x30 != (type & 0x30)) {
    39	            length += ((type & 0x30) ^ 0x30) << 4;
    40	            type |= 0x30;
    41	        }
    42	        switch (MySQLBinaryColumnType.valueOf(type)) {
    43	            case ENUM:
    44	                return readEnumValue(length, payload);
    45	            case SET:
    46	                return payload.getByteBuf().readByte();
    47	            case STRING:
    48	                return new MySQLBinaryString(payload.readStringFixByBytes(readActualLength(length, payload)));
    49	            default:
    50	                throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(MySQLBinaryColumnType.valueOf(type).toString());
    51	        }
    52	    }
    53	    
    54	    private int readActualLength(final int length, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    55	        return length < 256 ? payload.getByteBuf().readUnsignedByte() : payload.getByteBuf().readUnsignedShortLE();
    56	    }
    57	    
    58	    private Serializable readEnumValue(final int meta, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    59	        switch (meta) {
    60	            case 1:
    61	                return payload.readInt1();
    62	            case 2:
    63	                return payload.readInt2();
    64	            default:
    65	                throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.format("MySQL Enum meta in binlog only include value 1 or 2, but actual is %s", meta));
    66	        }
    67	    }
    68	}

2026-05-30 04:40:41,273 - INFO - swea-agent-apache__shardingsphere-38622 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now let me focus on the JSON value decoder. The key lines are:

- Line 93: `throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));` in `decodeValue`
- Line 184: `throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));` in `decodeValueEntry`
- Line 204: `throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(inlineValue));` in `outputLiteral`

The error says "Unsupported SQL operation: 4". Looking at the code:
- Type 4 = `JsonValueTypes.LITERAL` (0x04)

In `decodeValue`, type 4 (LITERAL) is NOT handled! Let me check again:

```java
switch (type) {
    case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT: // 0x00
    case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT: // 0x01
    case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:  // 0x02
    case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:  // 0x03
    case JsonValueTypes.INT16:             // 0x05
    case JsonValueTypes.UINT16:            // 0x06
    case JsonValueTypes.INT32:             // 0x07
    case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:            // 0x08
    case JsonValueTypes.INT64:             // 0x09
    case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:            // 0x0a
    case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:            // 0x0b
    case JsonValueTypes.STRING:            // 0x0c
        ...
    default:
        throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));
}
```

**Yes! `LITERAL` (0x04) and `CUSTOM_DATA` (0x0f) are missing from the `decodeValue` switch!**

And in `decodeValueEntry`, LITERAL IS handled:
```java
case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
    outputLiteral(getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall), stringBuilder);
    break;
```

So when a JSON value is a literal (null, true, false), `decodeValueEntry` handles it properly. But when the top-level JSON value is a literal, `decodeValue` doesn't handle it.

Now, actually, let me think about this. When you INSERT `'null'` into a JSON column, MySQL should store it as a JSON string "null" (type 0x0c STRING), not as a JSON null literal (type 0x04). 

But wait - the error says "Unsupported SQL operation: 4". Let me re-examine...

Actually, looking at the MySQL source more carefully, when you use `INSERT INTO ... VALUES('null')`, the string 'null' is a SQL string literal that gets parsed as JSON. The JSON parser would interpret this as the JSON value `null` (the literal null, not the string "null"). So MySQL would store this as a JSON literal null (type 0x04).

But then the error would happen at line 93 in `decodeValue`, because type 4 (LITERAL) is not handled there!

However, if the JSON is an object or array containing a null, it would be fine because `decodeValueEntry` handles LITERAL. Only when the entire JSON value is just a literal (like `null`, `true`, or `false`) would the top-level `decodeValue` fail.

But the PR description says the error occurs with `'null'` as a string. Let me re-read...

Actually, rethinking: the SQL `INSERT INTO reproduce_json_parse_error(settlement_assets) VALUES('null');` inserts the string 'null'. MySQL's JSON parser interprets 'null' as the JSON literal null value (not the string "null"). So the stored JSON binary value would be of type 0x04 (LITERAL) with inline value 0 (LITERAL_NULL). This would hit the `decodeValue` method at the top level, which doesn't handle type 0x04.

BUT WAIT: the same would apply if you insert `VALUES('true')` or `VALUES('false')` or `VALUES('123')`. Actually, `VALUES('123')` would be stored as INT64 or something. But `VALUES('null')`, `VALUES('true')`, `VALUES('false')` would all be stored as LITERAL type.

So the fix should be to add handling for `LITERAL` type in `decodeValue` method.

But also, what about `CUSTOM_DATA` (0x0f)? That should probably also be handled (or at least not throw an exception that corrupts the binlog parsing).

Let me also check for `OPAQUE` values. According to MySQL source, 0x0f is `OPAQUE` which is used for custom data types. But for now, let's focus on the reported issue.

Let me look at the test files to understand better

    49

    54	    @Test
    55	    void assertDecodeSmallJsonObjectWithLiteral() {
    56	        List<Object[]> jsonEntries = new LinkedList<>();
    57	        jsonEntries.add(new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.LITERAL, "key1", JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_NULL});
    58	        jsonEntries.add(new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.LITERAL, "key2", JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_TRUE});
    59	        jsonEntries.add(new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.LITERAL, "key3", JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_FALSE});
    60	        ByteBuf payload = mockJsonObjectByteBuf(jsonEntries, true);
    61	        assertThat(MySQLJsonValueDecoder.decode(payload), is("{\"key1\":null,\"key2\":true,\"key3\":false}"));
    62	    }

    68	        jsonEntries.add(new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.LITERAL, "key2", JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_TRUE});
    69	        jsonEntries.add(new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.LITERAL, "key3", JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_FALSE});

   128	    
   129	    private ByteBuf mockJsonObjectByteBuf(final List<Object[]> jsonEntries, final boolean isSmall) {
   130	        ByteBuf result = Unpooled.buffer();
   131	        result.writeByte(isSmall ? JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT : JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT);
   132	        result.writeBytes(mockJsonObjectByteBufValue(jsonEntries, isSmall));
   133	        return result;
   134	    }
   135	    
   136	    private ByteBuf mockJsonObjectByteBufValue(final List<Object[]> jsonEntries, final boolean isSmall) {
   137	        ByteBuf result = Unpooled.buffer();
   138	        writeInt(result, jsonEntries.size(), isSmall);
   139	        writeInt(result, 0, isSmall);
   140	        int startOffset = isSmall
   141	                ? 1 + SMALL_JSON_INT_LENGTH + SMALL_JSON_INT_LENGTH + jsonEntries.size() * SMALL_JSON_KEY_META_DATA_LENGTH + jsonEntries.size() * SMALL_JSON_VALUE_META_DATA_LENGTH - 1
   142	                : 1 + LARGE_JSON_INT_LENGTH + LARGE_JSON_INT_LENGTH + jsonEntries.size() * LARGE_JSON_KEY_META_DATA_LENGTH + jsonEntries.size() * LARGE_JSON_VALUE_META_DATA_LENGTH - 1;
   143	        ByteBuf keyByteBuf = writeKeys(result, jsonEntries, startOffset, isSmall);
   144	        startOffset += keyByteBuf.readableBytes();
   145	        ByteBuf valueByteBuf = writeValues(result, jsonEntries, startOffset, isSmall);
   146	        result.writeBytes(keyByteBuf);
   147	        result.writeBytes(valueByteBuf);
   148	        return result;
   149	    }
   150	    
   151	    private ByteBuf mockJsonArrayByteBuf(final List<Object[]> jsonEntries, final boolean isSmall) {
   152	        ByteBuf result = Unpooled.buffer();
   153	        result.writeByte(isSmall ? JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY : JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY);
   154	        result.writeBytes(mockJsonArrayByteBufValue(jsonEntries, isSmall));
   155	        return result;
   156	    }
   157	    
   158	    private ByteBuf mockJsonArrayByteBufValue(final List<Object[]> jsonEntries, final boolean isSmall) {
   159	        ByteBuf result = Unpooled.buffer();
   160	        writeInt(result, jsonEntries.size(), isSmall);
   161	        writeInt(result, 0, isSmall);
   162	        int startOffset = isSmall
   163	                ? 1 + SMALL_JSON_INT_LENGTH + SMALL_JSON_INT_LENGTH + jsonEntries.size() * SMALL_JSON_VALUE_META_DATA_LENGTH - 1
   164	                : 1 + LARGE_JSON_INT_LENGTH + LARGE_JSON_INT_LENGTH + jsonEntries.size() * LARGE_JSON_VALUE_META_DATA_LENGTH - 1;
   165	        ByteBuf valueByteBuf = writeValues(result, jsonEntries, startOffset, isSmall);
   166	        result.writeBytes(valueByteBuf);
   167	        return result;
   168	    }
   169	    
   170	    private void writeInt(final ByteBuf jsonByteBuf, final int value, final boolean isSmall) {
   171	        if (isSmall) {
   172	            jsonByteBuf.writeShortLE(value);
   173	        } else {
   174	            jsonByteBuf.writeIntLE(value);
   175	        }
   176	    }
   177	    
   178	    private ByteBuf writeKeys(final ByteBuf jsonByteBuf, final List<Object[]> jsonEntries, final int startOffset, final boolean isSmall) {
   179	        ByteBuf result = Unpooled.buffer();
   180	        for (Object[] each : jsonEntries) {
   181	            writeInt(jsonByteBuf, startOffset + result.readableBytes(), isSmall);
   182	            byte[] keyBytes = ((String) each[1]).getBytes();
   183	            jsonByteBuf.writeShortLE(keyBytes.length);
   184	            result.writeBytes(keyBytes);
   185	        }
   186	        return result;
   187	    }
   188	    
   189	    private ByteBuf writeValues(final ByteBuf jsonByteBuf, final List<Object[]> jsonEntries, final int startOffset, final boolean isSmall) {
   190	        ByteBuf result = Unpooled.buffer();
   191	        for (Object[] each : jsonEntries) {
   192	            jsonByteBuf.writeByte((byte) each[0]);
   193	            int offsetOrInlineValue = getOffsetOrInlineValue(startOffset, result.readableBytes(), each, isSmall);
   194	            writeInt(jsonByteBuf, offsetOrInlineValue, isSmall);
   195	            writeValueToByteBuf(each, result, isSmall);
   196	        }
   197	        return result;
   198	    }
   199	    
   200	    private int getOffsetOrInlineValue(final int startOffset, final int readableBytes, final Object[] jsonEntry, final boolean isSmall) {
   201	        switch ((byte) jsonEntry[0]) {
   202	            case JsonValueTypes.INT16:
   203	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT16:
   204	                return (int) jsonEntry[2];
   205	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
   206	                return (byte) jsonEntry[2];
   207	            case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
   208	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
   209	                return isSmall ? startOffset + readableBytes : (int) jsonEntry[2];
   210	            default:
   211	                return startOffset + readableBytes;
   212	        }
   213	    }
   214	    
   215	    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   216	    private void writeValueToByteBuf(final Object[] jsonEntry, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final boolean isSmall) {
   217	        switch ((byte) jsonEntry[0]) {
   218	            case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT:
   219	                byteBuf.writeBytes(mockJsonObjectByteBufValue((List<Object[]>) jsonEntry[2], true));
   220	                break;
   221	            case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT:
   222	                byteBuf.writeBytes(mockJsonObjectByteBufValue((List<Object[]>) jsonEntry[2], false));
   223	                break;
   224	            case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:
   225	                byteBuf.writeBytes(mockJsonArrayByteBufValue((List<Object[]>) jsonEntry[2], true));
   226	                break;
   227	            case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:
   228	                byteBuf.writeBytes(mockJsonArrayByteBufValue((List<Object[]>) jsonEntry[2], false));
   229	                break;
   230	            case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
   231	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
   232	                if (isSmall) {
   233	                    byteBuf.writeIntLE((int) jsonEntry[2]);
   234	                }
   235	                break;
   236	            case JsonValueTypes.INT64:
   237	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:
   238	                byteBuf.writeLongLE((long) jsonEntry[2]);
   239	                break;
   240	            case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:
   241	                byteBuf.writeDoubleLE((double) jsonEntry[2]);
   242	                break;
   243	            case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
   244	                writeString(byteBuf, (String) jsonEntry[2]);
   245	                break;
   246	            default:
   247	        }
   248	    }
   249	    
   250	    private void writeString(final ByteBuf jsonByteBuf, final String value) {
   251	        byte[] result = codecDataLength(value.length());
   252	        jsonByteBuf.writeBytes(result, 0, result.length);
   253	        jsonByteBuf.writeBytes(value.getBytes());
   254	    }
   255	    
   256	    private byte[] codecDataLength(final int length) {
   257	        byte[] lengthData = new byte[32 / 7 + (0 == 32 % 7 ? 0 : 1)];
   258	        for (int i = 0; i < lengthData.length; i++) {
   259	            lengthData[i] = (byte) ((length >> (7 * i)) & 0x7f);
   260	        }
   261	        int index = lengthData.length - 1;
   262	        while (index > 0) {
   263	            if (0 != lengthData[index]) {
   264	                break;
   265	            }
   266	            index--;
   267	        }
   268	        for (int i = 0; i < index; i++) {
   269	            lengthData[i] |= 0x80;
   270	        }
   271	        byte[] result = new byte[index + 1];
   272	        System.arraycopy(lengthData, 0, result, 0, index + 1);
   273	        return result;
   274	    }
   275	    
   276	    private static Stream<Arguments> decodeTopLevelScalarArguments() {
   277	        return Stream.of(
   278	                Arguments.of("decode int16 top-level", mockTopLevelInt16ByteBuf(), "-32768"),
   279	                Arguments.of("decode uint16 top-level", mockTopLevelUInt16ByteBuf(), "65535"),
   280	                Arguments.of("decode string with escaped chars", mockTopLevelStringByteBuf(), "\"a\\\"\\\\b\""));
   281	    }
   282	    
   283	    private static Stream<Arguments> decodeUnsupportedArguments() {
   284	        MySQLJsonValueDecoderTest test = new MySQLJsonValueDecoderTest();
   285	        return Stream.of(
   286	                Arguments.of("throw unsupported exception for top-level custom type", mockUnsupportedTopLevelTypeByteBuf()),
   287	                Arguments.of("throw unsupported exception for value entry custom type",
   288	                        test.mockJsonObjectByteBuf(Collections.singletonList(new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.CUSTOM_DATA, "key1", 1}), true)),
   289	                Arguments.of("throw unsupported exception for literal inline value",
   290	                        test.mockJsonObjectByteBuf(Collections.singletonList(new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.LITERAL, "key1", (byte) 3}), true)));
   291	    }
   292	    
   293	    private static Stream<Arguments> decodeObjectWithInlineNumberArguments() {
   294	        return Stream.of(
   295	                Arguments.of("decode small object with int16", true, JsonValueTypes.INT16, 0x00007fff, 0x00008000, "{\"key1\":32767,\"key2\":-32768}"),
   296	                Arguments.of("decode large object with int16", false, JsonValueTypes.INT16, 0x00007fff, 0x00008000, "{\"key1\":32767,\"key2\":-32768}"),
   297	                Arguments.of("decode small object with uint16", true, JsonValueTypes.UINT16, 0x00007fff, 0x00008000, "{\"key1\":32767,\"key2\":32768}"),
   298	                Arguments.of("decode large object with uint16", false, JsonValueTypes.UINT16, 0x00007fff, 0x00008000, "{\"key1\":32767,\"key2\":32768}"),
   299	                Arguments.of("decode small object with int32", true, JsonValueTypes.INT32, Integer.MAX_VALUE, Integer.MIN_VALUE, "{\"key1\":2147483647,\"key2\":-2147483648}"),
   300	                Arguments.of("decode large object with int32", false, JsonValueTypes.INT32, Integer.MAX_VALUE, Integer.MIN_VALUE, "{\"key1\":2147483647,\"key2\":-2147483648}"),
   301	                Arguments.of("decode small object with uint32", true, JsonValueTypes.UINT32, Integer.MAX_VALUE, Integer.MIN_VALUE, "{\"key1\":2147483647,\"key2\":2147483648}"),
   302	                Arguments.of("decode large object with uint32", false, JsonValueTypes.UINT32, Integer.MAX_VALUE, Integer.MIN_VALUE, "{\"key1\":2147483647,\"key2\":2147483648}"));
   303	    }
   304	    
   305	    private static Stream<Arguments> decodeSmallJsonObjectWithNonInlineTypeArguments() {
   306	        String value1 = "";
   307	        String value2 = Strings.repeat("1", (int) (Math.pow(2D, 7D) - 1D));
   308	        String value3 = Strings.repeat("1", (int) (Math.pow(2D, 7D) - 1D + 1D));
   309	        String value4 = Strings.repeat("1", (int) (Math.pow(2D, 14D) - 1D));
   310	        return Stream.of(
   311	                Arguments.of("decode small object with int64", Arrays.asList(new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.INT64, "key1", Long.MAX_VALUE}, new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.INT64, "key2", Long.MIN_VALUE}),
   312	                        "{\"key1\":9223372036854775807,\"key2\":-9223372036854775808}"),
   313	                Arguments.of("decode small object with uint64", Arrays.asList(new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.UINT64, "key1", Long.MAX_VALUE}, new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.UINT64, "key2", Long.MIN_VALUE}),
   314	                        "{\"key1\":9223372036854775807,\"key2\":9223372036854775808}"),
   315	                Arguments.of("decode small object with double", Arrays.asList(new Object[][]{new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE, "key1", Double.MAX_VALUE}}),
   316	                        "{\"key1\":1.7976931348623157E308}"),
   317	                Arguments.of("decode small object with string",
   318	                        Arrays.asList(new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.STRING, "key1", value1}, new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.STRING, "key2", value2}, new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.STRING, "key3", value3},
   319	                                new Object[]{JsonValueTypes.STRING, "key4", value4}),
   320	                        String.format("{\"key1\":\"%s\",\"key2\":\"%s\",\"key3\":\"%s\",\"key4\":\"%s\"}", value1, value2, value3, value4)));
   321	    }
   322	    
   323	    private static Stream<Arguments> decodeNestedJsonArguments() {
   324	        return Stream.of(
   325	                Arguments.of("decode small object with sub json", true, JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT, "key1", "{\"subJson\":{\"key1\":111}}"),
   326	                Arguments.of("decode large object with sub json", false, JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT, "key1", "{\"subJson\":{\"key1\":111}}"),
   327	                Arguments.of("decode small object with sub array", true, JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY, null, "{\"subJson\":[111]}"));
   328	    }
   329

Now I understand fully. Looking at the test:

1. `decodeTopLevelScalarArguments` tests INT16, UINT16, and STRING at the top level - but NOT LITERAL, INT32, UINT32, INT64, UINT64, or DOUBLE.

2. `decodeUnsupportedArguments` tests that `CUSTOM_DATA` (0x0f) at top level throws an exception, and that `CUSTOM_DATA` as value entry throws an exception, and that literal inline value 3 throws an exception (since only 0, 1, 2 are valid literals).

Now the issue: The `decodeValue` method doesn't handle:
- `LITERAL` (0x04)
- `DOUBLE` (0x0b)

Wait, DOUBLE (0x0b) is also not in the `decodeValue` switch! Neither is INT32, UINT32, INT64, UINT64.

But looking at the test `decodeTopLevelScalarArguments`, it only tests INT16, UINT16, and STRING at top level. So it seems like the top-level decoder was intentionally limited.

Now, the PR description says the error occurs with `'null'` which would be stored as LITERAL null. The fix should add LITERAL handling to `decodeValue`.

But also, for completeness, we should probably add handling for all the scalar types that are missing from `decodeValue`: LITERAL, INT32, UINT32, INT64, UINT64, DOUBLE. However, the PR description specifically mentions the issue with 'null' (LITERAL type). Let me focus on that.

Actually, let me reconsider. When you INSERT `'null'` into a JSON column, MySQL's JSON type stores this as a JSON literal null. The binlog would contain:
- Type byte: 0x04 (LITERAL)
- Followed by the inline value (0 for null)

But `decodeValue` doesn't handle type 0x04, so it falls to default and throws `UnsupportedSQLOperationException("4")`.

Let me also check the `decodeValue` method more carefully. For top-level scalars like INT16, UINT16, STRING, they read inline data. For LITERAL, the inline data would be just the literal value (0, 1, or 2).

    25	import java.io.Serializable;
    26	import java.math.BigInteger;
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * JSON type value decoder for MySQL.
    30	 *
    31	 * @see <a href="https://github.com/mysql/mysql-server/blob/5.7/sql/json_binary.h">json_binary</a>
    32	 */
    33	@NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PRIVATE)
    34	public final class MySQLJsonValueDecoder {
    35	    
    36	    private static final BigInteger MAX_BIG_INTEGER_VALUE = new BigInteger("18446744073709551615");
    37	    
    38	    /**
    39	     * Decode mysql json binary data to json string.
    40	     *
    41	     * @param byteBuf json binary value payload
    42	     * @return json string
    43	     */
    44	    public static Serializable decode(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
    45	        int valueType = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte() & 0xff;
    46	        StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
    47	        decodeValue(valueType, 1, byteBuf, result);
    48	        return result.toString();
    49	    }
    50	    
    51	    private static void decodeValue(final int type, final int offset, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
    52	        int oldOffset = byteBuf.readerIndex();
    53	        byteBuf.readerIndex(offset);
    54	        try {
    55	            switch (type) {
    56	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT:
    57	                    decodeJsonObject(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    58	                    break;
    59	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT:
    60	                    decodeJsonObject(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    61	                    break;
    62	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:
    63	                    decodeJsonArray(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    64	                    break;
    65	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:
    66	                    decodeJsonArray(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    67	                    break;
    68	                case JsonValueTypes.INT16:
    69	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readShortLE());
    70	                    break;
    71	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT16:
    72	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE());
    73	                    break;
    74	                case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
    75	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readIntLE());
    76	                    break;
    77	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
    78	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE());
    79	                    break;
    80	                case JsonValueTypes.INT64:
    81	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readLongLE());
    82	                    break;
    83	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:
    84	                    stringBuilder.append(readUnsignedLongLE(byteBuf));
    85	                    break;
    86	                case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:
    87	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readDoubleLE());
    88	                    break;
    89	                case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
    90	                    outputString(decodeString(byteBuf.slice()), stringBuilder);
    91	                    break;
    92	                default:
    93	                    throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));
    94	            }
    95	        } finally {
    96	            byteBuf.readerIndex(oldOffset);
    97	        }
    98	    }
    99	    
   100	    private static BigInteger readUnsignedLongLE(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {

- 0x01 LARGE_JSON_OBJECT

- 0x08 UINT32

- 0x0a UINT64
- 0x0b DOUBLE
- 0x0c STRING

But it's MISSING:
- 0x04 LITERAL

And also 0x0f CUSTOM_DATA/OPAQUE.

Now the fix: I need to add `LITERAL` handling to `decodeValue`. For a top-level LITERAL, the next byte (at the offset) is the inline value (0 for null, 1 for true, 2 for false).

Let me also check: in `decodeValueEntry`, when handling `LITERAL`, it uses `getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall)` to get the inline value. But for top-level `decodeValue`, there's no "isSmall" concept - we just need to read a byte.

Actually, looking at the binary format more carefully: in `decodeValue`, the offset is 1 (right after the type byte). For a top-level literal, the inline value should be at position 1 (one byte). But wait, `getIntBasedObjectSize` reads either 2 bytes (small) or 4 bytes (large). For top-level, we just need to read 1 byte.

Let me look at the MySQL source code for JSON binary format to understand how top-level scalar values are encoded.

Actually, looking at how INT16 is handled at top level:
- Type byte: 0x05
- Then 2 bytes of the int16 value

And UINT16:
- Type byte: 0x06
- Then 2 bytes of the uint16 value

And STRING:
- Type byte: 0x0c
- Then variable-length encoded length + string bytes

For LITERAL:
- Type byte: 0x04
- Then 1 byte of the literal value (0, 1, or 2)

So for top-level LITERAL, we just need to read one byte and pass it to `outputLiteral`. The fix should be:

```java
case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
    outputLiteral(byteBuf.readUnsignedByte(), stringBuilder);
    break;
```

This suggests that the exception causes the parser to not properly skip the bytes it was supposed to read, leading to corruption. The fix to `decodeValue` will prevent the exception from being thrown in the first place.

import io.netty.buffer.ByteBuf;
import io.netty.buffer.Unpooled;

public class TestJsonDecode {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        // Test top-level LITERAL null (type 0x04 with value 0)
        byte[] data = new byte[] { 0x04, 0x00 };
        ByteBuf buf = Unpooled.wrappedBuffer(data);
        // Call the decode method via reflection since it's package-private
        Class<?> clazz = Class.forName("org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.value.string.MySQLJsonValueDecoder");
        java.lang.reflect.Method method = clazz.getMethod("decode", ByteBuf.class);
        try {
            Object result = method.invoke(null, buf);
            System.out.println("SUCCESS: " + result);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            System.out.println("ERROR: " + e.getCause().getMessage());
            e.getCause().printStackTrace();
        }
    }
}
EOF

    18	package org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.value.string;
    19	
    20	import io.netty.buffer.ByteBuf;
    21	import lombok.AccessLevel;
    22	import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
    23	import org.apache.shardingsphere.infra.exception.generic.UnsupportedSQLOperationException;
    24	
    25	import java.io.Serializable;
    26	import java.math.BigInteger;
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * JSON type value decoder for MySQL.
    30	 *
    31	 * @see <a href="https://github.com/mysql/mysql-server/blob/5.7/sql/json_binary.h">json_binary</a>
    32	 */
    33	@NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PRIVATE)
    34	public final class MySQLJsonValueDecoder {
    35	    
    36	    private static final BigInteger MAX_BIG_INTEGER_VALUE = new BigInteger("18446744073709551615");
    37	    
    38	    /**
    39	     * Decode mysql json binary data to json string.
    40	     *
    41	     * @param byteBuf json binary value payload
    42	     * @return json string
    43	     */
    44	    public static Serializable decode(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
    45	        int valueType = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte() & 0xff;
    46	        StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
    47	        decodeValue(valueType, 1, byteBuf, result);
    48	        return result.toString();
    49	    }
    50	    
    51	    private static void decodeValue(final int type, final int offset, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
    52	        int oldOffset = byteBuf.readerIndex();
    53	        byteBuf.readerIndex(offset);
    54	        try {
    55	            switch (type) {
    56	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT:
    57	                    decodeJsonObject(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    58	                    break;
    59	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT:
    60	                    decodeJsonObject(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    61	                    break;
    62	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:
    63	                    decodeJsonArray(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    64	                    break;
    65	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:
    66	                    decodeJsonArray(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    67	                    break;
    68	                case JsonValueTypes.INT16:
    69	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readShortLE());
    70	                    break;
    71	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT16:
    72	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE());
    73	                    break;
    74	                case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
    75	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readIntLE());
    76	                    break;
    77	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
    78	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE());
    79	                    break;
    80	                case JsonValueTypes.INT64:
    81	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readLongLE());
    82	                    break;
    83	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:
    84	                    stringBuilder.append(readUnsignedLongLE(byteBuf));
    85	                    break;
    86	                case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:
    87	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readDoubleLE());
    88	                    break;
    89	                case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
    90	                    outputLiteral(byteBuf.readUnsignedByte(), stringBuilder);
    91	                    break;
    92	                case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
    93	                    outputString(decodeString(byteBuf.slice()), stringBuilder);
    94	                    break;
    95	                default:
    96	                    throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));
    97	            }
    98	        } finally {
    99	            byteBuf.readerIndex(oldOffset);
   100	        }

   197	    
   198	    private static void outputLiteral(final int inlineValue, final StringBuilder out) {
   199	        switch (inlineValue) {
   200	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_NULL:
   201	                out.append("null");
   202	                break;
   203	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_TRUE:
   204	                out.append("true");
   205	                break;
   206	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_FALSE:
   207	                out.append("false");
   208	                break;
   209	            default:
   210	                throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(inlineValue));
   211	        }
   212	    }
   213	    
   214	    private static String decodeString(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   215	        int length = decodeDataLength(byteBuf);
   216	        byte[] buffer = new byte[length];
   217	        byteBuf.readBytes(buffer, 0, length);
   218	        return new String(buffer);
   219	    }
   220	    
   221	    private static int decodeDataLength(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   222	        int result = 0;
   223	        int i = 0;
   224	        while (true) {
   225	            int data = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte();
   226	            result |= (data & 0x7f) << (7 * i);
   227	            if (0 == (data & 0x80)) {
   228	                break;
   229	            }
   230	            i++;
   231	        }
   232	        return result;
   233	    }
   234	    
   235	    private static void outputString(final String str, final StringBuilder out) {
   236	        out.append('"');
   237	        for (int i = 0; i < str.length(); ++i) {
   238	            char c = str.charAt(i);
   239	            if (c == '"' || c == '\\') {
   240	                out.append('\\');
   241	            }
   242	            out.append(c);
   243	        }
   244	        out.append('"');
   245	    }
   246	    
   247	    /**
   248	     * Json value types.
   249	     */
   250	    @NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PRIVATE)
   251	    public static final class JsonValueTypes {
   252	        
   253	        public static final byte SMALL_JSON_OBJECT = 0x00;
   254	        
   255	        public static final byte LARGE_JSON_OBJECT = 0x01;
   256	        
   257	        public static final byte SMALL_JSON_ARRAY = 0x02;
   258	        
   259	        public static final byte LARGE_JSON_ARRAY = 0x03;
   260	        
   261	        /**
   262	         * Literal(true/false/null).
   263	         */
   264	        public static final byte LITERAL = 0x04;
   265	        
   266	        public static final byte LITERAL_NULL = 0x00;
   267	        
   268	        public static final byte LITERAL_TRUE = 0x01;
   269	        
   270	        public static final byte LITERAL_FALSE = 0x02;
   271

    18	package org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.value.string;
    19	
    20	import io.netty.buffer.ByteBuf;
    21	import lombok.AccessLevel;
    22	import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
    23	import org.apache.shardingsphere.infra.exception.generic.UnsupportedSQLOperationException;
    24	
    25	import java.io.Serializable;
    26	import java.math.BigInteger;
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * JSON type value decoder for MySQL.
    30	 *
    31	 * @see <a href="https://github.com/mysql/mysql-server/blob/5.7/sql/json_binary.h">json_binary</a>
    32	 */
    33	@NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PRIVATE)
    34	public final class MySQLJsonValueDecoder {
    35	    
    36	    private static final BigInteger MAX_BIG_INTEGER_VALUE = new BigInteger("18446744073709551615");
    37	    
    38	    /**
    39	     * Decode mysql json binary data to json string.
    40	     *
    41	     * @param byteBuf json binary value payload
    42	     * @return json string
    43	     */
    44	    public static Serializable decode(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
    45	        int valueType = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte() & 0xff;
    46	        StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
    47	        decodeValue(valueType, 1, byteBuf, result);
    48	        return result.toString();
    49	    }
    50	    
    51	    private static void decodeValue(final int type, final int offset, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
    52	        int oldOffset = byteBuf.readerIndex();
    53	        byteBuf.readerIndex(offset);
    54	        try {
    55	            switch (type) {
    56	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT:
    57	                    decodeJsonObject(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    58	                    break;
    59	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT:
    60	                    decodeJsonObject(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    61	                    break;
    62	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:
    63	                    decodeJsonArray(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    64	                    break;
    65	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:
    66	                    decodeJsonArray(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    67	                    break;
    68	                case JsonValueTypes.INT16:
    69	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readShortLE());
    70	                    break;
    71	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT16:
    72	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE());
    73	                    break;
    74	                case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
    75	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readIntLE());
    76	                    break;
    77	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
    78	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE());
    79	                    break;
    80	                case JsonValueTypes.INT64:
    81	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readLongLE());
    82	                    break;
    83	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:
    84	                    stringBuilder.append(readUnsignedLongLE(byteBuf));
    85	                    break;
    86	                case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:
    87	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readDoubleLE());
    88	                    break;
    89	                case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
    90	                    outputLiteral(byteBuf.readUnsignedByte(), stringBuilder);
    91	                    break;
    92	                case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
    93	                    outputString(decodeString(byteBuf.slice()), stringBuilder);
    94	                    break;
    95	                default:
    96	                    throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));
    97	            }
    98	        } finally {
    99	            byteBuf.readerIndex(oldOffset);
   100	        }
   101	    }
   102	    
   103	    private static BigInteger readUnsignedLongLE(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   104	        long value = byteBuf.readLongLE();
   105	        return 0L <= value ? BigInteger.valueOf(value) : MAX_BIG_INTEGER_VALUE.add(BigInteger.valueOf(1L + value));
   106	    }
   107	    
   108	    private static void decodeJsonObject(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
   109	        stringBuilder.append('{');
   110	        int count = getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   111	        getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   112	        String[] keys = new String[count];
   113	        for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   114	            keys[i] = decodeKeyEntry(isSmall, byteBuf);
   115	        }
   116	        for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   117	            if (0 < i) {
   118	                stringBuilder.append(',');
   119	            }
   120	            stringBuilder.append('"').append(keys[i]).append("\":");
   121	            decodeValueEntry(isSmall, byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   122	        }
   123	        stringBuilder.append('}');
   124	    }
   125	    
   126	    private static void decodeJsonArray(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
   127	        stringBuilder.append('[');
   128	        int count = getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   129	        getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   130	        for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   131	            if (0 < i) {
   132	                stringBuilder.append(',');
   133	            }
   134	            decodeValueEntry(isSmall, byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   135	        }
   136	        stringBuilder.append(']');
   137	    }
   138	    
   139	    private static String decodeKeyEntry(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   140	        int offset = getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   141	        int length = byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE();
   142	        byte[] data = new byte[length];
   143	        byteBuf.getBytes(offset, data, 0, length);
   144	        return new String(data);
   145	    }
   146	    
   147	    private static void decodeValueEntry(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
   148	        int type = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte() & 0xff;
   149	        switch (type) {
   150	            case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT:
   151	            case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT:
   152	            case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:
   153	            case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:
   154	            case JsonValueTypes.INT64:
   155	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:
   156	            case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:
   157	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
   158	                    outputLiteral(byteBuf.readUnsignedByte(), stringBuilder);
   159	                    break;
   160	                case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
   161	                decodeValue(type, getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   162	                break;
   163	            case JsonValueTypes.INT16:
   164	                stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readShortLE());
   165	                if (!isSmall) {
   166	                    byteBuf.skipBytes(2);
   167	                }
   168	                break;
   169	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT16:
   170	                stringBuilder.append(getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall));
   171	                break;
   172	            case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
   173	                if (isSmall) {
   174	                    decodeValue(type, byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE(), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   175	                } else {
   176	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readIntLE());
   177	                }
   178	                break;
   179	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
   180	                if (isSmall) {
   181	                    decodeValue(type, byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE(), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   182	                } else {
   183	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE());
   184	                }
   185	                break;
   186	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
   187	                outputLiteral(getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall), stringBuilder);
   188	                break;
   189	            default:
   190	                throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));
   191	        }
   192	    }
   193	    
   194	    private static int getIntBasedObjectSize(final ByteBuf byteBuf, final boolean isSmall) {
   195	        return isSmall ? byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE() : (int) byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE();
   196	    }

    18	package org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.value.string;
    19	
    20	import io.netty.buffer.ByteBuf;
    21	import lombok.AccessLevel;
    22	import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
    23	import org.apache.shardingsphere.infra.exception.generic.UnsupportedSQLOperationException;
    24	
    25	import java.io.Serializable;
    26	import java.math.BigInteger;
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * JSON type value decoder for MySQL.
    30	 *
    31	 * @see <a href="https://github.com/mysql/mysql-server/blob/5.7/sql/json_binary.h">json_binary</a>
    32	 */
    33	@NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PRIVATE)
    34	public final class MySQLJsonValueDecoder {
    35	    
    36	    private static final BigInteger MAX_BIG_INTEGER_VALUE = new BigInteger("18446744073709551615");
    37	    
    38	    /**
    39	     * Decode mysql json binary data to json string.
    40	     *
    41	     * @param byteBuf json binary value payload
    42	     * @return json string
    43	     */
    44	    public static Serializable decode(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
    45	        int valueType = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte() & 0xff;
    46	        StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
    47	        decodeValue(valueType, 1, byteBuf, result);
    48	        return result.toString();
    49	    }
    50	    
    51	    private static void decodeValue(final int type, final int offset, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
    52	        int oldOffset = byteBuf.readerIndex();
    53	        byteBuf.readerIndex(offset);
    54	        try {
    55	            switch (type) {
    56	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT:
    57	                    decodeJsonObject(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    58	                    break;
    59	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT:
    60	                    decodeJsonObject(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    61	                    break;
    62	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:
    63	                    decodeJsonArray(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    64	                    break;
    65	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:
    66	                    decodeJsonArray(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    67	                    break;
    68	                case JsonValueTypes.INT16:
    69	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readShortLE());
    70	                    break;
    71	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT16:
    72	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE());
    73	                    break;
    74	                case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
    75	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readIntLE());
    76	                    break;
    77	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
    78	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE());
    79	                    break;
    80	                case JsonValueTypes.INT64:
    81	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readLongLE());
    82	                    break;
    83	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:
    84	                    stringBuilder.append(readUnsignedLongLE(byteBuf));
    85	                    break;
    86	                case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:
    87	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readDoubleLE());
    88	                    break;
    89	                case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
    90	                    outputString(decodeString(byteBuf.slice()), stringBuilder);
    91	                    break;
    92	                default:
    93	                    throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));
    94	            }
    95	        } finally {
    96	            byteBuf.readerIndex(oldOffset);
    97	        }
    98	    }
    99	    
   100	    private static BigInteger readUnsignedLongLE(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   101	        long value = byteBuf.readLongLE();
   102	        return 0L <= value ? BigInteger.valueOf(value) : MAX_BIG_INTEGER_VALUE.add(BigInteger.valueOf(1L + value));
   103	    }
   104	    
   105	    private static void decodeJsonObject(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
   106	        stringBuilder.append('{');
   107	        int count = getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   108	        getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   109	        String[] keys = new String[count];
   110	        for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   111	            keys[i] = decodeKeyEntry(isSmall, byteBuf);
   112	        }
   113	        for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   114	            if (0 < i) {
   115	                stringBuilder.append(',');
   116	            }
   117	            stringBuilder.append('"').append(keys[i]).append("\":");
   118	            decodeValueEntry(isSmall, byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   119	        }
   120	        stringBuilder.append('}');
   121	    }
   122	    
   123	    private static void decodeJsonArray(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
   124	        stringBuilder.append('[');
   125	        int count = getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   126	        getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   127	        for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   128	            if (0 < i) {
   129	                stringBuilder.append(',');
   130	            }
   131	            decodeValueEntry(isSmall, byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   132	        }
   133	        stringBuilder.append(']');
   134	    }
   135	    
   136	    private static String decodeKeyEntry(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   137	        int offset = getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall);
   138	        int length = byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE();
   139	        byte[] data = new byte[length];
   140	        byteBuf.getBytes(offset, data, 0, length);
   141	        return new String(data);
   142	    }
   143	    
   144	    private static void decodeValueEntry(final boolean isSmall, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
   145	        int type = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte() & 0xff;
   146	        switch (type) {
   147	            case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT:
   148	            case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT:
   149	            case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:
   150	            case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:
   151	            case JsonValueTypes.INT64:
   152	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:
   153	            case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:
   154	            case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
   155	                decodeValue(type, getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   156	                break;
   157	            case JsonValueTypes.INT16:
   158	                stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readShortLE());
   159	                if (!isSmall) {
   160	                    byteBuf.skipBytes(2);
   161	                }
   162	                break;
   163	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT16:
   164	                stringBuilder.append(getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall));
   165	                break;
   166	            case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
   167	                if (isSmall) {
   168	                    decodeValue(type, byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE(), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   169	                } else {
   170	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readIntLE());
   171	                }
   172	                break;
   173	            case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
   174	                if (isSmall) {
   175	                    decodeValue(type, byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE(), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
   176	                } else {
   177	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE());
   178	                }
   179	                break;
   180	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
   181	                outputLiteral(getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall), stringBuilder);
   182	                break;
   183	            default:
   184	                throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));
   185	        }
   186	    }
   187	    
   188	    private static int getIntBasedObjectSize(final ByteBuf byteBuf, final boolean isSmall) {
   189	        return isSmall ? byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE() : (int) byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE();
   190	    }
   191	    
   192	    private static void outputLiteral(final int inlineValue, final StringBuilder out) {
   193	        switch (inlineValue) {
   194	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_NULL:
   195	                out.append("null");
   196	                break;
   197	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_TRUE:
   198	                out.append("true");
   199	                break;
   200	            case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL_FALSE:
   201	                out.append("false");
   202	                break;
   203	            default:
   204	                throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(inlineValue));
   205	        }
   206	    }
   207	    
   208	    private static String decodeString(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   209	        int length = decodeDataLength(byteBuf);
   210	        byte[] buffer = new byte[length];
   211	        byteBuf.readBytes(buffer, 0, length);
   212	        return new String(buffer);
   213	    }
   214	    
   215	    private static int decodeDataLength(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
   216	        int result = 0;
   217	        int i = 0;
   218	        while (true) {
   219	            int data = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte();
   220	            result |= (data & 0x7f) << (7 * i);
   221	            if (0 == (data & 0x80)) {
   222	                break;
   223	            }
   224	            i++;
   225	        }
   226	        return result;
   227	    }
   228	    
   229	    private static void outputString(final String str, final StringBuilder out) {
   230	        out.append('"');
   231	        for (int i = 0; i < str.length(); ++i) {
   232	            char c = str.charAt(i);
   233	            if (c == '"' || c == '\\') {
   234	                out.append('\\');
   235	            }
   236	            out.append(c);
   237	        }
   238	        out.append('"');
   239	    }
   240	    
   241	    /**
   242	     * Json value types.
   243	     */
   244	    @NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PRIVATE)
   245	    public static final class JsonValueTypes {
   246	        
   247	        public static final byte SMALL_JSON_OBJECT = 0x00;
   248	        
   249	        public static final byte LARGE_JSON_OBJECT = 0x01;
   250	        
   251	        public static final byte SMALL_JSON_ARRAY = 0x02;
   252	        
   253	        public static final byte LARGE_JSON_ARRAY = 0x03;
   254	        
   255	        /**
   256	         * Literal(true/false/null).
   257	         */
   258	        public static final byte LITERAL = 0x04;
   259	        
   260	        public static final byte LITERAL_NULL = 0x00;
   261	        
   262	        public static final byte LITERAL_TRUE = 0x01;
   263

Good. Now I can see the original file correctly. The issue is:

1. In `decodeValue` (line 51-98): The LITERAL type (0x04) is NOT handled, so when a top-level JSON value is a literal (like 'null'), it throws `UnsupportedSQLOperationException("4")`.

2. In `decodeValueEntry` (line 144-186): LITERAL IS handled at line 180-182 correctly.

Now, looking at the test file `decodeTopLevelScalarArguments`, it tests INT16, UINT16, and STRING at top level but NOT LITERAL, DOUBLE, INT32, UINT32, INT64, or UINT64. But the PR description specifically mentions the 'null' issue, which is LITERAL.

However, I should also note that the PR description says:
> INSERT INTO reproduce_json_parse_error(settlement_assets) VALUES('null');

When you insert the string 'null' into a JSON column, MySQL parses this as the JSON literal `null`. The binary representation would be a single byte `0x04` followed by `0x00` (for null). Since `decodeValue` doesn't handle 0x04, it throws an exception.

But actually, I should also consider: what if someone inserts `'true'` or `'false'`? Those would also be LITERAL types. And what about `'123'` which would be an integer type that IS already handled? Those should work. But `'"null"'` (a JSON string containing "null") would be type STRING (0x0c) which is handled.

Now let me properly apply the fix. I need to add LITERAL handling to `decodeValue`:



🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/patch.py << 'EOF'
import sys

with open(sys.argv[1], 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Add LITERAL case before STRING in decodeValue
old = """                case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
                    outputString(decodeString(byteBuf.slice()), stringBuilder);
                    break;
                default:
                    throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));"""

new = """                case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
                    outputLiteral(byteBuf.readUnsignedByte(), stringBuilder);
                    break;
                case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
                    outputString(decodeString(byteBuf.slice()), stringBuilder);
                    break;
                default:
                    throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));"""

content = content.replace(old, new)

with open(sys.argv[1], 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)

print("Done")
EOF
