    18	package org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.value.string;
    19	
    20	import io.netty.buffer.ByteBuf;
    21	import lombok.AccessLevel;
    22	import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
    23	import org.apache.shardingsphere.infra.exception.generic.UnsupportedSQLOperationException;
    24	
    25	import java.io.Serializable;
    26	import java.math.BigInteger;
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * JSON type value decoder for MySQL.
    30	 *
    31	 * @see <a href="https://github.com/mysql/mysql-server/blob/5.7/sql/json_binary.h">json_binary</a>
    32	 */
    33	@NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PRIVATE)
    34	public final class MySQLJsonValueDecoder {
    35	    
    36	    private static final BigInteger MAX_BIG_INTEGER_VALUE = new BigInteger("18446744073709551615");
    37	    
    38	    /**
    39	     * Decode mysql json binary data to json string.
    40	     *
    41	     * @param byteBuf json binary value payload
    42	     * @return json string
    43	     */
    44	    public static Serializable decode(final ByteBuf byteBuf) {
    45	        int valueType = byteBuf.readUnsignedByte() & 0xff;
    46	        StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
    47	        decodeValue(valueType, 1, byteBuf, result);
    48	        return result.toString();
    49	    }
    50	    
    51	    private static void decodeValue(final int type, final int offset, final ByteBuf byteBuf, final StringBuilder stringBuilder) {
    52	        int oldOffset = byteBuf.readerIndex();
    53	        byteBuf.readerIndex(offset);
    54	        try {
    55	            switch (type) {
    56	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT:
    57	                    decodeJsonObject(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    58	                    break;
    59	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT:
    60	                    decodeJsonObject(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    61	                    break;
    62	                case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:
    63	                    decodeJsonArray(true, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    64	                    break;
    65	                case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:
    66	                    decodeJsonArray(false, byteBuf.slice(), stringBuilder);
    67	                    break;
    68	                case JsonValueTypes.INT16:
    69	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readShortLE());
    70	                    break;
    71	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT16:
    72	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE());
    73	                    break;
    74	                case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
    75	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readIntLE());
    76	                    break;
    77	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
    78	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readUnsignedIntLE());
    79	                    break;
    80	                case JsonValueTypes.INT64:
    81	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readLongLE());
    82	                    break;
    83	                case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:
    84	                    stringBuilder.append(readUnsignedLongLE(byteBuf));
    85	                    break;
    86	                case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:
    87	                    stringBuilder.append(byteBuf.readDoubleLE());
    88	                    break;
    89	                case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
    90	                    outputLiteral(byteBuf.readUnsignedByte(), stringBuilder);
    91	                    break;
    92	                case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
    93	                    outputString(decodeString(byteBuf.slice()), stringBuilder);
    94	                    break;
    95	                default:
    96	                    throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.valueOf(type));
    97	            }
    98	        } finally {
    99	            byteBuf.readerIndex(oldOffset);
   100	        }

    18	package org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row;
    19	
    20	import lombok.Getter;
    21	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.constant.MySQLBinaryColumnType;
    22	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.AbstractMySQLBinlogEventPacket;
    23	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.MySQLBinlogEventHeader;
    24	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.MySQLBinlogColumnDef;
    25	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.command.query.binary.execute.MySQLNullBitmap;
    26	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.payload.MySQLPacketPayload;
    27	
    28	import java.util.LinkedList;
    29	import java.util.List;
    30	
    31	/**
    32	 * MySQL binlog table map event packet.
    33	 *
    34	 * @see <a href="https://dev.mysql.com/doc/dev/mysql-server/latest/classbinary__log_1_1Table__map__event.html">TABLE_MAP_EVENT</a>
    35	 */
    36	@Getter
    37	public final class MySQLBinlogTableMapEventPacket extends AbstractMySQLBinlogEventPacket {
    38	    
    39	    private final long tableId;
    40	    
    41	    private final int flags;
    42	    
    43	    private final String schemaName;
    44	    
    45	    private final String tableName;
    46	    
    47	    private final int columnCount;
    48	    
    49	    private final List<MySQLBinlogColumnDef> columnDefs;
    50	    
    51	    private final MySQLNullBitmap nullBitMap;
    52	    
    53	    public MySQLBinlogTableMapEventPacket(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    54	        super(binlogEventHeader);
    55	        tableId = payload.readInt6();
    56	        flags = payload.readInt2();
    57	        schemaName = payload.readStringFix(payload.readInt1());
    58	        payload.skipReserved(1);
    59	        tableName = payload.readStringFix(payload.readInt1());
    60	        payload.skipReserved(1);
    61	        columnCount = (int) payload.readIntLenenc();
    62	        columnDefs = new LinkedList<>();
    63	        readColumnDefs(payload);
    64	        readColumnMetaDefs(payload);
    65	        nullBitMap = new MySQLNullBitmap(columnCount, payload);
    66	        // mysql 8 binlog table map event include column type def
    67	        // for support lower than 8, read column type def by sql query
    68	        // so skip readable bytes here
    69	        int remainBytesLength = getRemainBytesLength(payload);
    70	        if (remainBytesLength > 0) {
    71	            payload.skipReserved(remainBytesLength);
    72	        }
    73	    }
    74	    
    75	    private void readColumnDefs(final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    76	        for (int i = 0; i < columnCount; i++) {
    77	            columnDefs.add(new MySQLBinlogColumnDef(MySQLBinaryColumnType.valueOf(payload.readInt1())));
    78	        }
    79	    }
    80	    
    81	    private void readColumnMetaDefs(final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    82	        payload.readIntLenenc();
    83	        for (MySQLBinlogColumnDef each : columnDefs) {
    84	            each.setColumnMeta(readColumnMetaDef(each.getColumnType(), payload));
    85	        }
    86	    }
    87	    
    88	    private int readColumnMetaDef(final MySQLBinaryColumnType columnType, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    89	        switch (columnType) {
    90	            case STRING:
    91	            case DECIMAL:
    92	            case NEWDECIMAL:
    93	                return payload.getByteBuf().readUnsignedShort();
    94	            case BIT:
    95	            case VAR_STRING:
    96	            case VARCHAR:
    97	            case ENUM:
    98	                return payload.readInt2();
    99	            case BLOB:
   100	            case TINY_BLOB:
   101	            case DOUBLE:
   102	            case FLOAT:
   103	            case TIME2:
   104	            case TIMESTAMP2:
   105	            case DATETIME2:
   106	            case JSON:
   107	                return payload.readInt1();
   108	            default:
   109	                return 0;
   110	        }
   111	    }
   112	    
   113	    @Override
   114	    protected void writeEvent(final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   115	    }
   116	}

    18	package org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.client.netty;
    19	
    20	import io.netty.buffer.ByteBuf;
    21	import io.netty.buffer.ByteBufUtil;
    22	import io.netty.channel.ChannelHandlerContext;
    23	import io.netty.handler.codec.ByteToMessageDecoder;
    24	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    25	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.core.exception.PipelineInternalException;
    26	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.MySQLBinlogContext;
    27	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.MySQLBaseBinlogEvent;
    28	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.PlaceholderBinlogEvent;
    29	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.query.MySQLQueryBinlogEvent;
    30	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.rows.MySQLDeleteRowsBinlogEvent;
    31	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.rows.MySQLUpdateRowsBinlogEvent;
    32	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.rows.MySQLWriteRowsBinlogEvent;
    33	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.transaction.MySQLXidBinlogEvent;
    34	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.constant.CommonConstants;
    35	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.constant.MySQLBinlogEventType;
    36	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.MySQLBinlogEventHeader;
    37	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.management.MySQLBinlogFormatDescriptionEventPacket;
    38	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.management.MySQLBinlogRotateEventPacket;
    39	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.MySQLBinlogRowsEventPacket;
    40	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.MySQLBinlogTableMapEventPacket;
    41	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.payload.MySQLPacketPayload;
    42	
    43	import java.util.LinkedList;
    44	import java.util.List;
    45	import java.util.Map;
    46	import java.util.Optional;
    47	
    48	/**
    49	 * MySQL binlog event packet decoder.
    50	 */
    51	@Slf4j
    52	public final class MySQLBinlogEventPacketDecoder extends ByteToMessageDecoder {
    53	    
    54	    private static final String TX_BEGIN_SQL = "BEGIN";
    55	    
    56	    private final MySQLBinlogContext binlogContext;
    57	    
    58	    private final boolean decodeWithTX;
    59	    
    60	    private List<MySQLBaseBinlogEvent> records = new LinkedList<>();
    61	    
    62	    public MySQLBinlogEventPacketDecoder(final int checksumLength, final Map<Long, MySQLBinlogTableMapEventPacket> tableMap, final boolean decodeWithTX) {
    63	        this.decodeWithTX = decodeWithTX;
    64	        binlogContext = new MySQLBinlogContext(checksumLength, tableMap);
    65	    }
    66	    
    67	    @Override
    68	    protected void decode(final ChannelHandlerContext ctx, final ByteBuf in, final List<Object> out) {
    69	        while (in.readableBytes() >= 1 + MySQLBinlogEventHeader.MYSQL_BINLOG_EVENT_HEADER_LENGTH) {
    70	            in.markReaderIndex();
    71	            MySQLPacketPayload payload = new MySQLPacketPayload(in, ctx.channel().attr(CommonConstants.CHARSET_ATTRIBUTE_KEY).get());
    72	            checkPayload(payload);
    73	            MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader = new MySQLBinlogEventHeader(payload, binlogContext.getChecksumLength());
    74	            if (!checkEventIntegrity(in, binlogEventHeader)) {
    75	                return;
    76	            }
    77	            Optional<MySQLBaseBinlogEvent> binlogEvent = decodeEvent(binlogEventHeader, payload);
    78	            if (!binlogEvent.isPresent()) {
    79	                skipChecksum(binlogEventHeader.getEventType(), in);
    80	                return;
    81	            }
    82	            if (binlogEvent.get() instanceof PlaceholderBinlogEvent) {
    83	                out.add(binlogEvent.get());
    84	                skipChecksum(binlogEventHeader.getEventType(), in);
    85	                return;
    86	            }
    87	            if (decodeWithTX) {
    88	                processEventWithTX(binlogEvent.get(), out);
    89	            } else {
    90	                processEventIgnoreTX(binlogEvent.get(), out);
    91	            }
    92	            skipChecksum(binlogEventHeader.getEventType(), in);
    93	        }
    94	    }
    95	    
    96	    private void checkPayload(final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    97	        int statusCode = payload.readInt1();
    98	        if (255 == statusCode) {
    99	            int errorNo = payload.readInt2();
   100	            payload.skipReserved(1);
   101	            String sqlState = payload.readStringFix(5);
   102	            throw new PipelineInternalException("Decode binlog event failed, errorCode: %d, sqlState: %s, errorMessage: %s", errorNo, sqlState, payload.readStringEOF());
   103	        }
   104	        if (0 != statusCode) {
   105	            log.debug("Illegal binlog status code {}, remaining packet \n{}", statusCode, readRemainPacket(payload));
   106	        }
   107	    }
   108	    
   109	    private String readRemainPacket(final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   110	        return ByteBufUtil.hexDump(payload.readStringFixByBytes(payload.getByteBuf().readableBytes()));
   111	    }
   112	    
   113	    private boolean checkEventIntegrity(final ByteBuf in, final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader) {
   114	        if (in.readableBytes() < binlogEventHeader.getEventSize() - MySQLBinlogEventHeader.MYSQL_BINLOG_EVENT_HEADER_LENGTH) {
   115	            log.debug("the event body is not complete, event size={}, readable bytes={}", binlogEventHeader.getEventSize(), in.readableBytes());
   116	            in.resetReaderIndex();
   117	            return false;
   118	        }
   119	        return true;
   120	    }
   121	    
   122	    private void processEventWithTX(final MySQLBaseBinlogEvent binlogEvent, final List<Object> out) {
   123	        if (binlogEvent instanceof MySQLQueryBinlogEvent) {
   124	            MySQLQueryBinlogEvent queryEvent = (MySQLQueryBinlogEvent) binlogEvent;
   125	            if (TX_BEGIN_SQL.equals(queryEvent.getSql())) {
   126	                records = new LinkedList<>();
   127	            } else {
   128	                out.add(binlogEvent);
   129	            }
   130	        } else if (binlogEvent instanceof MySQLXidBinlogEvent) {
   131	            records.add(binlogEvent);
   132	            out.add(records);
   133	        } else {
   134	            records.add(binlogEvent);
   135	        }
   136	    }
   137	    
   138	    private void processEventIgnoreTX(final MySQLBaseBinlogEvent binlogEvent, final List<Object> out) {
   139	        if (binlogEvent instanceof MySQLQueryBinlogEvent) {
   140	            MySQLQueryBinlogEvent queryEvent = (MySQLQueryBinlogEvent) binlogEvent;
   141	            if (TX_BEGIN_SQL.equals(queryEvent.getSql())) {
   142	                return;
   143	            }
   144	        }
   145	        out.add(binlogEvent);
   146	    }
   147	    
   148	    private Optional<MySQLBaseBinlogEvent> decodeEvent(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   149	        switch (MySQLBinlogEventType.valueOf(binlogEventHeader.getEventType()).orElse(MySQLBinlogEventType.UNKNOWN_EVENT)) {
   150	            case ROTATE_EVENT:
   151	                decodeRotateEvent(binlogEventHeader, payload);
   152	                return Optional.empty();
   153	            case FORMAT_DESCRIPTION_EVENT:
   154	                decodeFormatDescriptionEvent(binlogEventHeader, payload);
   155	                return Optional.empty();
   156	            case TABLE_MAP_EVENT:
   157	                decodeTableMapEvent(binlogEventHeader, payload);
   158	                return Optional.empty();
   159	            case WRITE_ROWS_EVENT_V1:
   160	            case WRITE_ROWS_EVENT_V2:
   161	                return Optional.of(decodeWriteRowsEventV2(binlogEventHeader, payload));
   162	            case UPDATE_ROWS_EVENT_V1:
   163	            case UPDATE_ROWS_EVENT_V2:
   164	                return Optional.of(decodeUpdateRowsEventV2(binlogEventHeader, payload));
   165	            case DELETE_ROWS_EVENT_V1:
   166	            case DELETE_ROWS_EVENT_V2:
   167	                return Optional.of(decodeDeleteRowsEventV2(binlogEventHeader, payload));
   168	            case QUERY_EVENT:
   169	                return Optional.of(decodeQueryEvent(binlogEventHeader, payload));
   170	            case XID_EVENT:
   171	                return Optional.of(decodeXidEvent(binlogEventHeader, payload));
   172	            default:
   173	                return Optional.of(decodePlaceholderEvent(binlogEventHeader, payload));
   174	        }
   175	    }
   176	    
   177	    private void decodeRotateEvent(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   178	        MySQLBinlogRotateEventPacket packet = new MySQLBinlogRotateEventPacket(binlogEventHeader, payload);
   179	        binlogContext.setFileName(packet.getNextBinlogName());
   180	    }
   181	    
   182	    private void decodeFormatDescriptionEvent(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   183	        MySQLBinlogFormatDescriptionEventPacket packet = new MySQLBinlogFormatDescriptionEventPacket(binlogEventHeader, payload);
   184	        // MySQL MGR checksum length is 0, but the event ends up with 4 extra bytes, need to skip them.
   185	        int readableBytes = payload.getByteBuf().readableBytes();
   186	        if (binlogEventHeader.getChecksumLength() <= 0 && readableBytes > 0) {
   187	            if (readableBytes != 4) {
   188	                log.warn("the format description event has extra bytes, readable bytes length={}, binlogEventHeader={}, formatDescriptionEvent={}", readableBytes, binlogEventHeader, packet);
   189	            }
   190	            payload.getByteBuf().skipBytes(readableBytes);
   191	        }
   192	    }
   193	    
   194	    private void decodeTableMapEvent(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   195	        binlogContext.putTableMapEvent(new MySQLBinlogTableMapEventPacket(binlogEventHeader, payload));
   196	    }
   197	    
   198	    private MySQLWriteRowsBinlogEvent decodeWriteRowsEventV2(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   199	        MySQLBinlogRowsEventPacket packet = new MySQLBinlogRowsEventPacket(binlogEventHeader, payload);
   200	        MySQLBinlogTableMapEventPacket tableMapEventPacket = binlogContext.getTableMapEvent(packet.getTableId());
   201	        packet.readRows(tableMapEventPacket, payload);
   202	        return new MySQLWriteRowsBinlogEvent(binlogContext.getFileName(),
   203	                binlogEventHeader.getLogPos(), binlogEventHeader.getTimestamp(), tableMapEventPacket.getSchemaName(), tableMapEventPacket.getTableName(), packet.getRows());
   204	    }
   205	    
   206	    private MySQLUpdateRowsBinlogEvent decodeUpdateRowsEventV2(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   207	        MySQLBinlogRowsEventPacket packet = new MySQLBinlogRowsEventPacket(binlogEventHeader, payload);
   208	        MySQLBinlogTableMapEventPacket tableMapEventPacket = binlogContext.getTableMapEvent(packet.getTableId());
   209	        packet.readRows(tableMapEventPacket, payload);
   210	        return new MySQLUpdateRowsBinlogEvent(binlogContext.getFileName(),
   211	                binlogEventHeader.getLogPos(), binlogEventHeader.getTimestamp(), tableMapEventPacket.getSchemaName(), tableMapEventPacket.getTableName(), packet.getRows(), packet.getRows2());
   212	    }
   213	    
   214	    private MySQLDeleteRowsBinlogEvent decodeDeleteRowsEventV2(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   215	        MySQLBinlogRowsEventPacket packet = new MySQLBinlogRowsEventPacket(binlogEventHeader, payload);
   216	        MySQLBinlogTableMapEventPacket tableMapEventPacket = binlogContext.getTableMapEvent(packet.getTableId());
   217	        packet.readRows(tableMapEventPacket, payload);
   218	        return new MySQLDeleteRowsBinlogEvent(binlogContext.getFileName(),
   219	                binlogEventHeader.getLogPos(), binlogEventHeader.getTimestamp(), tableMapEventPacket.getSchemaName(), tableMapEventPacket.getTableName(), packet.getRows());
   220	    }
   221	    
   222	    private PlaceholderBinlogEvent decodePlaceholderEvent(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   223	        PlaceholderBinlogEvent result = new PlaceholderBinlogEvent(binlogContext.getFileName(), binlogEventHeader.getLogPos(), binlogEventHeader.getTimestamp());
   224	        int remainDataLength = binlogEventHeader.getEventSize() + 1 - binlogEventHeader.getChecksumLength() - payload.getByteBuf().readerIndex();
   225	        if (remainDataLength > 0) {
   226	            payload.skipReserved(remainDataLength);
   227	        }
   228	        return result;
   229	    }
   230	    
   231	    private MySQLQueryBinlogEvent decodeQueryEvent(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   232	        int threadId = payload.readInt4();
   233	        int executionTime = payload.readInt4();
   234	        payload.skipReserved(1);
   235	        int errorCode = payload.readInt2();
   236	        payload.skipReserved(payload.readInt2());
   237	        String databaseName = payload.readStringNul();
   238	        String sql = payload.readStringFix(payload.getByteBuf().readableBytes() - binlogEventHeader.getChecksumLength());
   239	        return new MySQLQueryBinlogEvent(binlogContext.getFileName(), binlogEventHeader.getLogPos(), binlogEventHeader.getTimestamp(), threadId, executionTime, errorCode, databaseName, sql);
   240	    }
   241	    
   242	    private MySQLXidBinlogEvent decodeXidEvent(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   243	        return new MySQLXidBinlogEvent(binlogContext.getFileName(), binlogEventHeader.getLogPos(), binlogEventHeader.getTimestamp(), payload.readInt8());
   244	    }
   245	    
   246	    private void skipChecksum(final int eventType, final ByteBuf in) {
   247	        if (0 < binlogContext.getChecksumLength() && MySQLBinlogEventType.FORMAT_DESCRIPTION_EVENT.getValue() != eventType) {
   248	            in.skipBytes(binlogContext.getChecksumLength());
   249	        }
   250	    }
   251	}

    18	package org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row;
    19	
    20	import lombok.Getter;
    21	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.constant.MySQLBinlogEventType;
    22	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.AbstractMySQLBinlogEventPacket;
    23	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.MySQLBinlogEventHeader;
    24	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.MySQLBinlogColumnDef;
    25	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.binlog.row.column.value.MySQLBinlogProtocolValueFactory;
    26	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.packet.command.query.binary.execute.MySQLNullBitmap;
    27	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.protocol.mysql.payload.MySQLPacketPayload;
    28	
    29	import java.io.Serializable;
    30	import java.util.LinkedList;
    31	import java.util.List;
    32	
    33	/**
    34	 * MySQL binlog rows event packet.
    35	 *
    36	 * @see <a href="https://dev.mysql.com/doc/dev/mysql-server/latest/classbinary__log_1_1Rows__event.html">ROWS_EVENT</a>
    37	 * @see <a href="https://mariadb.com/kb/en/rows_event_v1v2-rows_compressed_event_v1/">ROWS_EVENT</a>
    38	 */
    39	@Getter
    40	public final class MySQLBinlogRowsEventPacket extends AbstractMySQLBinlogEventPacket {
    41	    
    42	    private final long tableId;
    43	    
    44	    private final int flags;
    45	    
    46	    private final int columnNumber;
    47	    
    48	    private final MySQLNullBitmap columnsPresentBitmap;
    49	    
    50	    private final MySQLNullBitmap columnsPresentBitmap2;
    51	    
    52	    private final List<Serializable[]> rows = new LinkedList<>();
    53	    
    54	    private final List<Serializable[]> rows2 = new LinkedList<>();
    55	    
    56	    public MySQLBinlogRowsEventPacket(final MySQLBinlogEventHeader binlogEventHeader, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    57	        super(binlogEventHeader);
    58	        tableId = payload.readInt6();
    59	        flags = payload.readInt2();
    60	        skipExtraData(payload);
    61	        columnNumber = (int) payload.readIntLenenc();
    62	        columnsPresentBitmap = new MySQLNullBitmap(columnNumber, payload);
    63	        columnsPresentBitmap2 = readUpdateColumnsPresentBitmap(payload);
    64	    }
    65	    
    66	    private void skipExtraData(final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    67	        if (isRowsEventVersion2(getBinlogEventHeader().getEventType())) {
    68	            int extraDataLength = payload.readInt2() - 2;
    69	            payload.skipReserved(extraDataLength);
    70	        }
    71	    }
    72	    
    73	    private boolean isRowsEventVersion2(final int eventType) {
    74	        return MySQLBinlogEventType.WRITE_ROWS_EVENT_V2.getValue() == eventType || MySQLBinlogEventType.UPDATE_ROWS_EVENT_V2.getValue() == eventType
    75	                || MySQLBinlogEventType.DELETE_ROWS_EVENT_V2.getValue() == eventType;
    76	    }
    77	    
    78	    private MySQLNullBitmap readUpdateColumnsPresentBitmap(final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    79	        return isUpdateRowsEvent(getBinlogEventHeader().getEventType()) ? new MySQLNullBitmap(columnNumber, payload) : null;
    80	    }
    81	    
    82	    private boolean isUpdateRowsEvent(final int eventType) {
    83	        return MySQLBinlogEventType.UPDATE_ROWS_EVENT_V2.getValue() == eventType || MySQLBinlogEventType.UPDATE_ROWS_EVENT_V1.getValue() == eventType;
    84	    }
    85	    
    86	    /**
    87	     * Read rows in binlog.
    88	     *
    89	     * @param tableMapEventPacket TABLE_MAP_EVENT packet before this ROWS_EVENT
    90	     * @param payload ROWS_EVENT packet payload
    91	     */
    92	    public void readRows(final MySQLBinlogTableMapEventPacket tableMapEventPacket, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    93	        List<MySQLBinlogColumnDef> columnDefs = tableMapEventPacket.getColumnDefs();
    94	        while (getRemainBytesLength(payload) > 0) {
    95	            rows.add(readRow(columnDefs, payload));
    96	            if (isUpdateRowsEvent(getBinlogEventHeader().getEventType())) {
    97	                rows2.add(readRow(columnDefs, payload));
    98	            }
    99	        }
   100	    }
   101	    
   102	    private Serializable[] readRow(final List<MySQLBinlogColumnDef> columnDefs, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   103	        MySQLNullBitmap nullBitmap = new MySQLNullBitmap(columnNumber, payload);
   104	        Serializable[] result = new Serializable[columnNumber];
   105	        for (int i = 0; i < columnNumber; i++) {
   106	            MySQLBinlogColumnDef columnDef = columnDefs.get(i);
   107	            result[i] = nullBitmap.isNullParameter(i) ? null : MySQLBinlogProtocolValueFactory.getBinlogProtocolValue(columnDef.getColumnType()).read(columnDef, payload);
   108	        }
   109	        return result;
   110	    }
   111	    
   112	    @Override
   113	    protected void writeEvent(final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
   114	    }
   115	}

I see. Now the key issue is that `readRows` (line 92-100) iterates while there are remaining bytes. If an exception is thrown during `readRow` (e.g., from the JSON decoder), the remaining bytes are NOT skipped, and the loop breaks. This could corrupt subsequent parsing.

But wait - if the exception is thrown, it would propagate up through `decodeWriteRowsEventV2`/`decodeUpdateRowsEventV2`/`decodeDeleteRowsEventV2` to `decodeEvent` and then to `decode` in `MySQLBinlogEventPacketDecoder`. There's no try-catch there, so the exception would propagate further up to the Netty pipeline.

However, the PR description says:
> "Current implementation attempts to skip the error event but fails to properly skip unresolved bytes"

This implies there IS some attempt to skip errors, but it fails. Let me search for where `UnsupportedSQLOperationException` is caught in the pipeline context.

    28	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.core.ingest.record.DataRecord;
    29	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.core.ingest.record.NormalColumn;
    30	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.core.ingest.record.PlaceholderRecord;
    31	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.core.ingest.record.Record;
    32	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.core.metadata.loader.PipelineTableMetaDataLoader;
    33	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.core.metadata.model.PipelineColumnMetaData;
    34	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.core.metadata.model.PipelineTableMetaData;
    35	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.data.MySQLBinlogDataHandler;
    36	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.MySQLBaseBinlogEvent;
    37	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.rows.MySQLBaseRowsBinlogEvent;
    38	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.rows.MySQLDeleteRowsBinlogEvent;
    39	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.rows.MySQLUpdateRowsBinlogEvent;
    40	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.event.rows.MySQLWriteRowsBinlogEvent;
    41	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.binlog.position.MySQLBinlogPosition;
    42	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.client.ConnectInfo;
    43	import org.apache.shardingsphere.data.pipeline.mysql.ingest.incremental.client.MySQLBinlogClient;
    44	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.connector.core.jdbcurl.parser.ConnectionProperties;
    45	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.connector.core.jdbcurl.parser.ConnectionPropertiesParser;
    46	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.connector.core.spi.DatabaseTypedSPILoader;
    47	import org.apache.shardingsphere.database.connector.core.type.DatabaseType;
    48	import org.apache.shardingsphere.infra.annotation.HighFrequencyInvocation;
    49	import org.apache.shardingsphere.infra.metadata.identifier.ShardingSphereIdentifier;
    50	import org.apache.shardingsphere.infra.spi.type.typed.TypedSPILoader;
    51	
    52	import java.io.Serializable;
    53	import java.util.Collections;
    54	import java.util.LinkedList;
    55	import java.util.List;
    56	import java.util.Objects;
    57	
    58	/**
    59	 * MySQL incremental dumper.
    60	 */
    61	@HighFrequencyInvocation
    62	@Slf4j
    63	public final class MySQLIncrementalDumper extends AbstractPipelineLifecycleRunnable implements IncrementalDumper {
    64	    
    65	    private final IncrementalDumperContext dumperContext;
    66	    
    67	    private final MySQLBinlogPosition binlogPosition;
    68	    
    69	    private final PipelineTableMetaDataLoader metaDataLoader;
    70	    
    71	    private final PipelineChannel channel;
    72	    
    73	    private final MySQLBinlogClient client;
    74	    
    75	    private final String catalog;
    76	    
    77	    public MySQLIncrementalDumper(final IncrementalDumperContext dumperContext, final IngestPosition binlogPosition, final PipelineChannel channel, final PipelineTableMetaDataLoader metaDataLoader) {
    78	        this.dumperContext = dumperContext;
    79	        this.binlogPosition = (MySQLBinlogPosition) binlogPosition;
    80	        this.channel = channel;
    81	        this.metaDataLoader = metaDataLoader;
    82	        StandardPipelineDataSourceConfiguration pipelineDataSourceConfig = (StandardPipelineDataSourceConfiguration) dumperContext.getCommonContext().getDataSourceConfig();
    83	        DatabaseType databaseType = TypedSPILoader.getService(DatabaseType.class, "MySQL");
    84	        ConnectionProperties connectionProps = DatabaseTypedSPILoader.getService(ConnectionPropertiesParser.class, databaseType).parse(pipelineDataSourceConfig.getUrl(), null, null);
    85	        ConnectInfo connectInfo = new ConnectInfo(
    86	                generateServerId(), connectionProps.getHostname(), connectionProps.getPort(), pipelineDataSourceConfig.getUsername(), pipelineDataSourceConfig.getPassword());
    87	        log.info("incremental dump, jdbcUrl={}, serverId={}, hostname={}, port={}", pipelineDataSourceConfig.getUrl(), connectInfo.getServerId(), connectInfo.getHost(), connectInfo.getPort());
    88	        client = new MySQLBinlogClient(connectInfo, dumperContext.isDecodeWithTX());
    89	        catalog = connectionProps.getCatalog();
    90	    }
    91	    
    92	    private int generateServerId() {
    93	        int result = hashCode();
    94	        return Integer.MIN_VALUE == result ? Integer.MAX_VALUE : Math.abs(result);
    95	    }
    96	    
    97	    @Override
    98	    protected void runBlocking() {
    99	        client.connect();
   100	        client.subscribe(binlogPosition.getFilename(), binlogPosition.getPosition());
   101	        while (isRunning()) {
   102	            handleEvents(client.poll());
   103	        }
   104	    }
   105	    
   106	    private void handleEvents(final List<MySQLBaseBinlogEvent> events) {
   107	        List<Record> dataRecords = new LinkedList<>();
   108	        for (MySQLBaseBinlogEvent each : events) {
   109	            dataRecords.addAll(handleEvent(each));
   110	        }
   111	        if (!dataRecords.isEmpty()) {
   112	            channel.push(dataRecords);
   113	        }
   114	    }
   115	    
   116	    private List<? extends Record> handleEvent(final MySQLBaseBinlogEvent event) {
   117	        if (!(event instanceof MySQLBaseRowsBinlogEvent)) {
   118	            return Collections.singletonList(createPlaceholderRecord(event));
   119	        }
   120	        MySQLBaseRowsBinlogEvent rowsEvent = (MySQLBaseRowsBinlogEvent) event;
   121	        if (!rowsEvent.getDatabaseName().equals(catalog) || !dumperContext.getCommonContext().getTableNameMapper().containsTable(rowsEvent.getTableName())) {
   122	            return Collections.singletonList(createPlaceholderRecord(event));
   123	        }
   124	        PipelineTableMetaData tableMetaData = getPipelineTableMetaData(rowsEvent.getTableName());
   125	        if (event instanceof MySQLWriteRowsBinlogEvent) {
   126	            return handleWriteRowsEvent((MySQLWriteRowsBinlogEvent) event, tableMetaData);
   127	        }
   128	        if (event instanceof MySQLUpdateRowsBinlogEvent) {
   129	            return handleUpdateRowsEvent((MySQLUpdateRowsBinlogEvent) event, tableMetaData);
   130	        }
   131	        if (event instanceof MySQLDeleteRowsBinlogEvent) {
   132	            return handleDeleteRowsEvent((MySQLDeleteRowsBinlogEvent) event, tableMetaData);
   133	        }
   134	        return Collections.emptyList();
   135	    }
   136	    
   137	    private PlaceholderRecord createPlaceholderRecord(final MySQLBaseBinlogEvent event) {
   138	        PlaceholderRecord result = new PlaceholderRecord(new MySQLBinlogPosition(event.getFileName(), event.getPosition()));
   139	        result.setCommitTime(event.getTimestamp() * 1000L);
   140	        return result;
   141	    }
   142	    
   143	    private PipelineTableMetaData getPipelineTableMetaData(final String actualTableName) {
   144	        ShardingSphereIdentifier logicTableName = dumperContext.getCommonContext().getTableNameMapper().getLogicTableName(actualTableName);
   145	        return metaDataLoader.getTableMetaData(dumperContext.getCommonContext().getTableAndSchemaNameMapper().getSchemaName(logicTableName), actualTableName);
   146	    }
   147	    
   148	    private List<DataRecord> handleWriteRowsEvent(final MySQLWriteRowsBinlogEvent event, final PipelineTableMetaData tableMetaData) {
   149	        List<DataRecord> result = new LinkedList<>();
   150	        for (Serializable[] each : event.getAfterRows()) {
   151	            DataRecord dataRecord = createDataRecord(PipelineSQLOperationType.INSERT, event, each.length);
   152	            for (int i = 0; i < each.length; i++) {
   153	                PipelineColumnMetaData columnMetaData = tableMetaData.getColumnMetaData(i + 1);
   154	                dataRecord.addColumn(new NormalColumn(columnMetaData.getName(), MySQLBinlogDataHandler.handle(columnMetaData, each[i]), true, columnMetaData.isUniqueKey()));
   155	            }
   156	            result.add(dataRecord);
   157	        }
   158	        return result;
   159	    }
   160	    
   161	    private List<DataRecord> handleUpdateRowsEvent(final MySQLUpdateRowsBinlogEvent event, final PipelineTableMetaData tableMetaData) {
   162	        List<DataRecord> result = new LinkedList<>();
   163	        for (int i = 0; i < event.getBeforeRows().size(); i++) {
   164	            Serializable[] beforeValues = event.getBeforeRows().get(i);
   165	            Serializable[] afterValues = event.getAfterRows().get(i);
   166	            DataRecord dataRecord = createDataRecord(PipelineSQLOperationType.UPDATE, event, beforeValues.length);
   167	            for (int j = 0; j < beforeValues.length; j++) {
   168	                PipelineColumnMetaData columnMetaData = tableMetaData.getColumnMetaData(j + 1);
   169	                Serializable oldValue = MySQLBinlogDataHandler.handle(columnMetaData, beforeValues[j]);
   170	                Serializable newValue = MySQLBinlogDataHandler.handle(columnMetaData, afterValues[j]);
   171	                boolean updated = !Objects.deepEquals(newValue, oldValue);
   172	                dataRecord.addColumn(new NormalColumn(columnMetaData.getName(), oldValue, newValue, updated, columnMetaData.isUniqueKey()));
   173	            }
   174	            result.add(dataRecord);
   175	        }
   176	        return result;
   177	    }
   178	    
   179	    private List<DataRecord> handleDeleteRowsEvent(final MySQLDeleteRowsBinlogEvent event, final PipelineTableMetaData tableMetaData) {
   180	        List<DataRecord> result = new LinkedList<>();
   181	        for (Serializable[] each : event.getBeforeRows()) {
   182	            DataRecord dataRecord = createDataRecord(PipelineSQLOperationType.DELETE, event, each.length);
   183	            for (int i = 0, length = each.length; i < length; i++) {
   184	                PipelineColumnMetaData columnMetaData = tableMetaData.getColumnMetaData(i + 1);
   185	                dataRecord.addColumn(new NormalColumn(columnMetaData.getName(), MySQLBinlogDataHandler.handle(columnMetaData, each[i]), null, true, columnMetaData.isUniqueKey()));
   186	            }
   187	            result.add(dataRecord);
   188	        }
   189	        return result;
   190	    }
   191	    
   192	    private DataRecord createDataRecord(final PipelineSQLOperationType type, final MySQLBaseRowsBinlogEvent rowsEvent, final int columnCount) {
   193	        String tableName = dumperContext.getCommonContext().getTableNameMapper().getLogicTableName(rowsEvent.getTableName()).toString();
   194	        IngestPosition binlogPosition = new MySQLBinlogPosition(rowsEvent.getFileName(), rowsEvent.getPosition());
   195	        DataRecord result = new DataRecord(type, tableName, binlogPosition, columnCount);
   196	        result.setActualTableName(rowsEvent.getTableName());
   197	        result.setCommitTime(rowsEvent.getTimestamp() * 1000L);
   198	        return result;
   199	    }
   200	    
   201	    @Override
   202	    protected void doStop() {
   203	        client.closeChannel(true);
   204	    }
   205	}

Now I can see: in `handleEvents` (line 106-114), it processes events. If an exception occurs during `handleEvent`, it would propagate out of `handleEvents`, out of `runBlocking`, and likely crash the dumper.

But actually, the issue is at a lower level. The exception happens during parsing (in `MySQLBinlogEventPacketDecoder.decode`), before it even reaches the dumper. Let me trace the flow:

1. `MySQLBinlogEventPacketDecoder.decode` calls `decodeEvent` 
2. `decodeEvent` calls `decodeWriteRowsEventV2` (or similar)
3. Which calls `MySQLBinlogRowsEventPacket.readRows`
4. Which calls `readRow`
5. Which calls `MySQLJsonBinlogProtocolValue.read`
6. Which calls `MySQLJsonValueDecoder.decode`
7. Which throws `UnsupportedSQLOperationException`

The exception is not caught anywhere in `MySQLBinlogEventPacketDecoder.decode`, so it propagates up to Netty, which would close the channel.

Now, the PR description says "Current implementation attempts to skip the error event but fails to properly skip unresolved bytes." This suggests there might be some error handling that attempts to skip, but it's not working correctly. However, looking at the code, I don't see such handling currently. Maybe the PR description is describing what SHOULD happen (the fix should skip unresolved bytes), not what currently happens.

Actually, re-reading the PR description more carefully:
> "When the parsing error occurs, the binlog client becomes corrupted"
> "Current implementation attempts to skip the error event but fails to properly skip unresolved bytes"
> "This causes incorrect parsing of subsequent events"

This might be describing a scenario where someone tried to fix this by catching the exception and skipping bytes, but that fix was incomplete. Or it could be describing the behavior of the `decodeValue` method: it reads the type byte, and for LITERAL type, it should read 1 more byte (the literal value), but instead it throws, leaving that byte unread. But `decodeValue` is called with `offset=1`, so the reader index is set to position 1 before the switch. If it throws, the `finally` block restores `oldOffset` (which is 0 after reading the type byte). So the byte at position 1 (the literal value) is indeed left unread.

But wait, in `decodeValue`, the offset is 1, and the reader is set to offset (1). Then for INT16, it reads 2 bytes (positions 1-2). For LITERAL, it should read 1 byte (position 1). If it throws, the reader is reset to `oldOffset` (which is 0). But the type byte at position 0 was already read by `decode()`. So the remaining bytes from position 1 onwards are "unresolved."

However, this happens inside `readRow` which is called in a loop that reads until remaining bytes are 0. If an exception is thrown mid-row, the remaining bytes of that row (and subsequent rows in the same event) are not consumed. This would corrupt the binlog parsing.

But my fix prevents the exception from being thrown in the first place for LITERAL type, which is the main issue described.

Let me also think about whether there's another layer of fix needed. Let me check if there's any exception handling in the `readRows` method or its callers.

Actually, looking at `readRows` again:

```java
public void readRows(final MySQLBinlogTableMapEventPacket tableMapEventPacket, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    List<MySQLBinlogColumnDef> columnDefs = tableMapEventPacket.getColumnDefs();
    while (getRemainBytesLength(payload) > 0) {
        rows.add(readRow(columnDefs, payload));
        if (isUpdateRowsEvent(getBinlogEventHeader().getEventType())) {
            rows2.add(readRow(columnDefs, payload));
        }
    }
}
```

There's no try-catch here. If `readRow` throws, the loop exits and the remaining bytes are not consumed. The exception propagates to `decodeWriteRowsEventV2` which doesn't catch it either.

The fix should ideally include exception handling that skips the problematic bytes. But the PR description only mentions the JSON column parse error with literal 'null'. My fix to `decodeValue` should resolve that specific issue.

However, to be safe, let me also check if there's any other place where the "4" (LITERAL type) could cause issues. Looking at `decodeValueEntry`, LITERAL is already handled correctly (line 180-182). So the only issue is in `decodeValue` for top-level scalar values.

Now let me also think about the `CUSTOM_DATA` (0x0f) type. The test `decodeUnsupportedArguments` expects `CUSTOM_DATA` to throw at both top-level and value-entry level. So that's intentionally unsupported. But if it occurs in real data, it would also cause corruption.

For now, let me focus on the minimal fix for the reported issue: adding LITERAL handling to `decodeValue`.

Let me also check if there's any issue with the `readRow` method that could cause problems even with the LITERAL fix. Looking at `readRow` again:

```java
private Serializable[] readRow(final List<MySQLBinlogColumnDef> columnDefs, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    MySQLNullBitmap nullBitmap = new MySQLNullBitmap(columnNumber, payload);
    Serializable[] result = new Serializable[columnNumber];
    for (int i = 0; i < columnNumber; i++) {
        MySQLBinlogColumnDef columnDef = columnDefs.get(i);
        result[i] = nullBitmap.isNullParameter(i) ? null : MySQLBinlogProtocolValueFactory.getBinlogProtocolValue(columnDef.getColumnType()).read(columnDef, payload);
    }
    return result;
}
```

If the column is NULL, it skips reading the value entirely (sets null). If the column is not NULL but is a JSON type, it calls `MySQLJsonBinlogProtocolValue.read()` which calls `MySQLJsonValueDecoder.decode()`. After my fix, for a literal null JSON value, it will properly return "null" string.

Now, let me also think about whether there's a need to handle `CUSTOM_DATA` (0x0f) in `decodeValue`. The test expects it to throw, but in production, if MySQL sends a JSON column with opaque data, it would still throw and corrupt the binlog. However, the PR description doesn't mention this, so I'll leave it as is.

Let me also verify my fix is correct by looking at how the test data is structured. The test `decodeTopLevelScalarArguments` tests top-level scalars:

- INT16: `{0x05, 0x00, 0x80}` → 32768 (as short LE) → "-32768"
- UINT16: `{0x05, 0xFF, 0xFF}` → wait, that's INT16. Let me recheck.

Actually looking at mock methods:
- `mockTopLevelInt16ByteBuf`: writes `JsonValueTypes.INT16` then `32768` as short LE → this reads as signed short = -32768
- `mockTopLevelUInt16ByteBuf`: writes `JsonValueTypes.UINT16` then `65535` as short LE → reads as unsigned short = 65535
- `mockTopLevelStringByteBuf`: writes `JsonValueTypes.STRING` then length + "a\"\\b"

So for LITERAL, the top-level format would be:
- `{0x04, 0x00}` → LITERAL null
- `{0x04, 0x01}` → LITERAL true
- `{0x04, 0x02}` → LITERAL false

My fix reads one unsigned byte after the type byte, which is correct for top-level literals.

Now, I should also consider another potential issue: the PR description mentions "parse binlog error when JSON column in increment task." The fix I made addresses the parsing of the JSON value itself. But could there also be an issue with how the binlog column meta is read for JSON columns?

Looking at `MySQLJsonBinlogProtocolValue.readLengthFromMeta`:
```java
private int readLengthFromMeta(final int columnMeta, final MySQLPacketPayload payload) {
    switch (columnMeta) {
        case 1:
            return payload.getByteBuf().readUnsignedByte();
        case 2:
            return payload.getByteBuf().readUnsignedShortLE();
        case 3:
            return payload.getByteBuf().readUnsignedMediumLE();
        case 4:
            return payload.readInt4();
        default:
            throw new UnsupportedSQLOperationException(String.format("MySQL JSON type meta in binlog should be range 1 to 4, but actual value is: %s", columnMeta));
    }
}
```

This reads the length of the JSON value based on the column meta. The column meta for JSON type is read in `MySQLBinlogTableMapEventPacket.readColumnMetaDef`:

```java
case JSON:
    return payload.readInt1();
```

So the column meta is 1 byte, and its value determines how many bytes to read for the length of the JSON data. According to MySQL documentation, the valid values are 1-4. If the meta value is something else (e.g., 0), this would also throw. But that's a different issue.

```java
case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_OBJECT:
case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_OBJECT:
case JsonValueTypes.SMALL_JSON_ARRAY:
case JsonValueTypes.LARGE_JSON_ARRAY:
case JsonValueTypes.INT64:
case JsonValueTypes.UINT64:
case JsonValueTypes.DOUBLE:
case JsonValueTypes.STRING:
    decodeValue(type, getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
    break;
```

And also for INT32 and UINT32 (small case):
```java
case JsonValueTypes.INT32:
    if (isSmall) {
        decodeValue(type, byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE(), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
    } else { ... }
    break;
case JsonValueTypes.UINT32:
    if (isSmall) {
        decodeValue(type, byteBuf.readUnsignedShortLE(), byteBuf, stringBuilder);
    } else { ... }
    break;
```

Notice that `LITERAL` is NOT among the types that call `decodeValue` in `decodeValueEntry`. Instead, it's handled directly:
```java
case JsonValueTypes.LITERAL:
    outputLiteral(getIntBasedObjectSize(byteBuf, isSmall), stringBuilder);
    break;
```

So `decodeValue` is only called for types where the data is at an offset (not inline). LITERAL is always inline, so `decodeValue` doesn't need to handle it for the value-entry case. But for the top-level case (called from `decode`), `decodeValue` is always called with offset=1, and LITERAL data is inline at that offset.

My fix correctly handles the top-level case by reading 1 byte (the literal value) directly from the current position.
